Tang Youren Explains Direct Sino-Japanese Negotiations; The Key to Diplomacy Lies Entirely in the Northeast Issue; Other Outstanding Cases Can Be Negotiated at Any Time 144

According to the Xin Xin News Agency, Tang Youren, Permanent Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, has been bedridden in Shanghai for nearly a month due to poisoning of his left middle finger. After treatment by Japanese doctor Yoshida, he has largely recovered. A reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency specially visited him at his residence on Ganstone Road yesterday and was granted an audience. According to him, his finger ailment has now largely recovered, but it will still take more than ten days for it to fully heal. However, as he is in charge of routine affairs, there are many matters that urgently need to be handled in Beijing. Therefore, he has now decided to return to Beijing by the end of this month to make some arrangements before returning to Shanghai for a short rest. Then, talking about Sino-Japanese diplomacy, the recent rumors circulating outside about direct Sino-Japanese negotiations are entirely a misunderstanding by the general public. Whether or not there are direct negotiations only refers to the Northeast issue. In the past, our country proposed that it be handled by the League of Nations because it did not want to negotiate directly with Japan. As for various other outstanding cases, there is always the possibility of negotiation at any time, regardless of whether it is direct or indirect. Later, when the reporter asked about Wang Yitang's trip to Japan, which was rumored to be for the restoration of the Huiye Bank, Tang replied that Wang's trip to Japan was entirely his personal action and he was not carrying any mission from the government. Because Wang is a Buddhist, he went to participate in a Buddhist conference. As for the Huiye Bank, its business has always been exclusively engaged in Sino-Japanese debt. However, our country cannot currently talk about repaying Japanese debt for the time being, so the bank has no way to recover at all.

Ji Zezin Discusses the Reasons for the Stagnant Sales of Chinese Tea; Commercial Decline and Heavy Dumping of Japanese Tea; We Must Strive to Recover by Improving the Quality of Our Tea 145

According to Ji Zezin, director of the Guidance Department of the International Trade Bureau, who spoke yesterday about the reasons for the stagnant sales of Chinese tea in the Nanyang region and the crisis of the tea industry, he spoke in great detail. The details are recorded below:

Decline of the Tea Market 146

According to his account, taking Singapore as an example, the Chinese tea industry used to be quite developed in the past. There were no fewer than forty or fifty to sixty or seventy tea merchants, large and small. However, in recent years, due to the economic downturn, the number has decreased to only twenty or thirty. The source of the tea is usually transported from Xiamen, Fuzhou, Wenzhou, and other places, and most of it is picked and roasted from Anxi and Wuyi Mountains. The best quality teas include famous varieties such as Seczhong, Qizhong, Tieguanyin, and Baimao Hou, followed by varieties such as Shuixian, Wulong, and Xueli. Anxi County alone produces tea leaves every year that are sold in Chaozhou, Zhangzhou, Tong'an, Xiamen, Nanyang, and other places, amounting to about two million yuan in national currency every year. Anxi has recently been plagued by many bandits, and the people are struggling to survive, so the tea production in the area has declined abnormally. However, this has a great impact on foreign trade and people's livelihoods.

Dumping of Taiwanese Tea 147

In recent years, the sales of Chinese tea in Malaya have gradually stagnated. Although the biggest reason is closely related to the global economic downturn, the competition from Taiwanese tea is the main reason. Taiwanese tea currently sells for only two, three, four, or five Straits dollars per box (one hundred packs, twenty-five catties each), while Chinese tea from Xiamen, Fuzhou, and Wenzhou must be above seven dollars. It is appropriate that Taiwanese tea wants to surpass Chinese tea. Japanese gold is currently extremely cheap. Although a box only sells for two, three, four, or five dollars in the Straits, it can earn four, five, seven, or eight dollars or more in Taiwan. Merchants who seek heavy profits, seeing the opportunity to profit, also abandon Chinese tea and replace it with Taiwanese tea. As a result, the future of Chinese tea is becoming increasingly bleak. Chinese tea has the harmony of the four seasons in China, and the tea leaves are picked around Qingming and Lixia, following the solar terms, so the aroma of Chinese tea is particularly good, different from that of other products. If the promotion is done properly, it may not be impossible to recover.

Heavy Tea Taxes 148

Another reason for the sluggish sales of Chinese tea is the tea tax levied by the Federated Malay States. It is necessary to pay eight cents per pound, and the tax on one box can reach more than two dollars and sixty cents. The same is true in the Dutch East Indies. Previously, the tax was only four guilders and eight cents per box, but now it is as much as six to eight or nine guilders. This increase in taxation is also a fatal blow to Chinese tea. In addition, during this time of economic downturn, tea merchants and shops have set up small carts along the streets to solicit customers in order to expand their business and maintain operations, which also shows the intensity of the competition.

Sharp Decline in Sales 149

The total number of tea imports into Malaya in 1933 has not yet been printed and published. The statistics for 1932, 1931, and 1930 are listed below to give a glimpse:

Imports from China: Weight/Value

1930: 4,704,780 lbs / 1,556,760 dollars

1931: 5,510,601 lbs / 1,065,149 dollars

1932: 3,590,990 lbs / 689,743 dollars

In 1932, tea imports into Malaya from China, Ceylon, Taiwan, and other places totaled 4,971,654 pounds, worth 1,196,582 dollars.

Further News on the Tianxiang Steamer Grounding and Sinking; Part of the Crew Can Arrive in Shanghai Today or Tomorrow; The Ship Has Not Completely Sunk and Six People Have Been Sent to Guard It 150

The Tianxiang Steamer of the Donggang Heji Company ran aground and sank on the morning of the 20th of this month near Nianzi Reef, near Beitongtou Mountain, off the coast of Wenzhou. Fortunately, the crew and passengers were all safely rescued and arrived in Ou. It is now heard that part of the crew will depart from Wenzhou to Shanghai. The following is the latest news obtained yesterday:

Crew Arrives in Shanghai 151

After the Tianxiang Steamer ran aground and sank on Nianzi Reef on the morning of the 20th due to thunderstorms, wind, and fog, the crew and passengers were rescued and arrived in Wen, temporarily housed in the Siming Guild Hall in the area as a reception center. The local Donggang Company received two telegrams the day before yesterday, but no telegram report yesterday. However, according to oral reports, part of the crew, led by the compradore Yang Zhiting, is taking a steamer from Wenzhou to Shanghai. If they take the Ping'an Company's Dahua Steamer, they can arrive this afternoon. If they take the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Haiyan Steamer, they can also arrive in Shanghai tomorrow afternoon. However, it is not certain which ship they are taking. As for the insurance company's compensation issue, it will be negotiated after the crew arrives in Shanghai and provides a detailed report.

People Sent to Guard 152

The ship sank at Nianzi Reef, under Beitongtou Mountain. Therefore, after the accident, the crew and passengers left the ship and first went to the mountain, and then hired fishing boats to go to Wenzhou. The shipowner saw that the stern of the ship had sunk, and the bow was still stranded on the rocks. The pilothouse could still be seen when the tide was high, and the bow could be seen three feet above the water after the tide receded. Therefore, before leaving the mountain for Ou, six crew members were sent to guard it, awaiting company orders. However, how the company will deal with the sunken ship depends on the insurance company that underwrote it.

Settlement Measures 153

The Tianxiang Steamer of the Donggang Heji Company has 30,000 yuan of peace insurance underwritten by the Joint Shipping Insurance Association. After the grounding, the company immediately reported to the insurance company. Now the Insurance Association has decided to wait for the crew to arrive in Shanghai to report before deciding on settlement measures based on the extent of the grounding. It is likely that they will give up salvage because the insurance amount is only 30,000 yuan, and salvage and repair may not be cost-effective.

China National Aviation Corporation Sends Personnel to Cixi to Claim the Pilot's Body; Plans to Find a Way to Transport It to Shanghai for Burial on a Scheduled Date; Notifies the Pilot's Family in the United States by Telegram 154

According to the Shishi News Agency, the China National Aviation Corporation's No. 17 aircraft has been missing for nearly a month. Yesterday, the company received a report that a body of a radio mechanic who was missing with the plane had been found in the waters off Zhejiang. This confirms that the people and the plane are all dead. The details are as follows:

Body Found 155

Since the loss of the plane, the China National Aviation Corporation has been constantly inquiring about the personnel who were missing with the plane. At 6:00 p.m. the day before yesterday, they suddenly received a telegram from Chen Baolin, the magistrate of Cixi County, stating that at dusk on the 20th, Shen A-da, a fisherman from Gaobishan, Shenshi Bridge, Cixi North, discovered a Western body while fishing. The body had been dead for a long time and was swollen and rotten all over. Several business cards with the words "A.M. Carlson, American Pacific Airlines, No. 3 Guangdong Road, Shanghai" were found on the body. After receiving the telegram, the company believed that the body was undoubtedly that of the radio mechanic Carlson (A.M. Carlson). They immediately dispatched Ling Yang last night, carrying funds, to take the Xinningxing Steamer to Zhejiang to collect the body and transport it to Shanghai. Carlson had only arrived in Shanghai two months before the loss of the plane. He was 30 years old and not yet married, so there are no family members in Shanghai.

Notification to the United States 156

The American pilot Garcia de la Torre and Carlson, who died on the No. 17 aircraft, had life insurance with a certain insurance company in the United States. Since the accident, the families of the three had requested telegrams to the United States proving their deaths so that they could receive the insurance amount. The Ministry had not replied immediately because the whereabouts of the pilot had not yet been found. The discovery of Carlson's body this time can definitively prove that the other crew members have also undoubtedly sunk into the sea. Therefore, after receiving a detailed report from the China National Aviation Corporation, it will send a telegram to the United States to formally prove that the pilots and others have indeed died in the plane crash. At the same time, the families of the deceased will be notified.

Ministry of Communications Forbids Ship Personnel from Serving Beyond Their Ranks; Various Shipping Companies Request Flexibility 160

Temporary Permission for First Mates to Serve as Captains on Ships Under 1,000 Tons; Shipping Guilds and Other Organizations Will Petition in Beijing Again; After the Ministry of Communications issued an order forbidding ship personnel from serving beyond their ranks, stipulating ship tonnage standards, implementing examination and verification for qualification, and setting a deadline of the end of June this year, otherwise their duties would be suspended, various shipping companies and shipping organizations in the city requested temporary flexibility from the Shipping Administration Bureau yesterday due to difficulties in handling. The details of the situation are recorded below:

Standards for Ship Personnel Service 161

Regarding the standards for ship personnel service for Chinese and foreign shipping companies, it is stipulated according to ship tonnage, divided into ocean routes, coastal routes, and inland river routes. Ships with a tonnage of more than 1,000 tons should have one captain, first mate, second mate, and chief engineer, etc. Ships with a tonnage of more than 500 tons and less than 1,000 tons should follow the same as above. However, shipping companies often hire qualified and experienced ship personnel as captains on ships with a tonnage of more than 1,000 tons, and the positions of the original first mate, second mate, and chief engineer are also uneven. The Ministry of Communications believes that this system has a great impact on the shipping industry, so it stipulates tonnage standards to prevent abuses and ensure safety.

Joint Request for Flexibility 162

At 2:00 p.m. tomorrow, representatives from the Shanghai Shipping Guild, the Marine Engineers General Guild, the Sanbei Company, the Dada Steamship Company, and other organizations will meet with Peng Hu, director of the Shipping Administration Bureau, to request flexibility in the standards for ship service before the deadline. Director Peng replied that the matter concerned orders from above and there was no room for flexibility. However, to take into account the difficulties of the shipping merchants, he replied to the representatives that ship personnel on ships with a tonnage of more than 1,000 tons should be handled according to the standards and should not serve beyond their ranks. On ships with a tonnage of more than 500 tons and less than 1,000 tons, first mates will be temporarily allowed to serve as captains, and second mates will be promoted to first mates before the deadline. Other chief engineers, etc., will also be appointed accordingly, as an expedient compromise. It is also heard that shipping guilds and other organizations will send representatives to Beijing to petition the Ministry of Communications in the coming days.

Zhou Yichun, president of Yenching University, recently came to Shanghai to negotiate important matters. Establishing Sub-Customs Stations in Qinhuangdao and Four Other Places; Revisions to the Measures for the Management of Civilian Vessels; Jianghaiguan Announced Yesterday for General Knowledge 164

The Ministry of Finance previously deemed it necessary to establish sub-customs stations in Qinhuangdao, Miaodao, Weihaiwei, and Shidao to manage civilian vessels, and drafted management measures, instructing Jianghaiguan to comply. It will be implemented from June 16th of this year. Jianghaiguan issued a notice yesterday announcing the revised measures for the management of civilian vessels. The notice states that the measures for the management of civilian vessels in Qinhuangdao, Miaodao, Weihaiwei, and Shidao sub-customs stations have been announced in the joint bulletin No. 1358. However, there are some amendments to be made to the original text of the measures. They are listed below: (A1) Civilian vessels sailing from Dalian Kwantung Leased Territory, the pseudo-Manchukuo, and foreign places to any coastal place between Qinhuangdao and Longkou should be changed to civilian vessels sailing from Dalian Kwantung Leased Territory to Manchukuo and a dotted line should be drawn eastward from Shidao to the Korean region north of Dongping. (A2) The words "Bohai Bay" should be changed to "Liaodong Bay." All civilian vessels are hereby notified. Supervisor Tang Hai'an.

Land Prices on West Yuhua Road Soar 169

North Sichuan Road has been known as the second Nanjing Road, because it is close to the central area and all kinds of conveniences are available. West Yuhua Road, which borders it to the north, is only four miles away from Nanjing Road and the Bund, which is closer than Yuyuan Road and Yidingpan Road in western Shanghai. Moreover, the width of the road, the quiet scenery, and the fresh air are better than those of Yuyuan Road and other places. In addition, water, electricity, and public utilities are all available, public buses run all day long, and transportation is extremely convenient. The residents nearby are either villas or public officials, teachers, students, and farmers, so it is very suitable for building houses and settling down. Before January 28th, the land price rose to 5,000 or 6,000 taels per mu. After the Shanghai Incident, the price once fell, but there were few sellers and transactions stagnated. Since the municipal government moved to the downtown area, land transactions in the area have become active. Recently, because Xinhua Bank has opened Xinhua Village in the middle of the road, it is heard that many wealthy businessmen and financial circles are building houses and settling down in the area, or buying large amounts of land to carry out similar plans. Therefore, land prices have soared, and there is a trend to restore the prices before January 28th. Recently, the land price has reached 4,500 taels to 5,000 taels per mu.

Shanghai Municipal Council Seeks Chinese Assistant Medical Officer 174

The Public Concession of the Shanghai Municipal Council, Health Department, currently has a vacancy for a Chinese Assistant Medical Officer (Chinese Assistant Medical Officer). Applicants must have considerable qualifications in internal and external medicine, be proficient in English, Mandarin, and local dialects, and be under 30 years old to be qualified (preferably unmarried). Applicants must first undergo a physical examination. After being selected, they must also undergo a six-month trial period before being officially employed. In terms of compensation, the starting monthly salary is 150 to 300 yuan, depending on qualifications. The highest salary in the future can reach 900 to 940 yuan. After five years of service, if recommended by the Director of the Health Department, the Municipal Council may send them to other places for further study. Applicants must submit a handwritten letter of application before June 11th, addressed to the Director of the Health Department, 223 Hankou Road, Shanghai Municipal Council. Applicants must not request an interview or seek assistance through connections, otherwise their qualifications will be cancelled. The selected personnel will start working around July 1st.

Zhou Songqian and Others Sue Tong Zhihe Case; Sentencing Scheduled for the 26th 175

Zhou Songqian and others, shareholders of the Chinese Light Bulb Factory on Xinzha Road in this city, sued Tong Zhihe and others in the Criminal Division of the Shanghai First Special District Court for embezzlement and breach of trust, alleging that Tong Zhihe and others had committed embezzlement and breach of trust. The plaintiffs stated that in October of the 21st year, they and the defendants jointly organized the Chinese Light Bulb Factory, appointing Tong Zhihe as manager and Sheng Henian as assistant manager. Since its opening, it has been quite successful. However, the defendants, intending to embezzle, colluded with shareholder Yu Yinda and others, and on March 7th of this year, Sheng Henian, Yu Yinda, and others issued a written document transferring the Chinese Light Bulb Factory, which the plaintiffs had invested in, to Tong Zhihe for continued operation, and all the shares held by the plaintiffs in the factory were discarded as waste paper. The defendants are representatives of the British American Tobacco factory workers.

Yesterday They Petitioned Party and Government Agencies; Today, Representatives of Two Factories Will Hold a Meeting to Discuss the Formation of a Strike Committee 176

According to Da Gong She, all the workers of the new British American Tobacco Company factory in Pudong, in order to help the unemployed workers of the old factory, declared a work stoppage a few days ago to urge the factory to realize the situation. The Fifth District Cigarette Workers' Union, considering that the labor unrest might be difficult to resolve and to avoid the expansion of disputes, yesterday sent representatives to petition the party and government separately, and decided to hold a workers' representative meeting of the two factories today to discuss the formation of a strike committee. The situation yesterday is recorded as follows:

(Petitioning Party and Government) In order to seek the prompt resumption of work at the old British American Tobacco factory, the Fifth District Cigarette Workers' Union specially sent Chen Peide, Lou Jingguan, and 37 others as representatives to petition the party and government agencies at 9:00 AM yesterday, first going to the Municipal Government, where Secretary-General Yu received them. After the labor representatives explained the situation in detail, Yu negotiated with the British American Tobacco Company. They then went to the Social Affairs Bureau to petition, where Secretary Li received them and gave a similar reply. Finally, they went to the Municipal Party Headquarters to petition, where Committee Member Wu Kaixian received them. The labor representatives demanded that the Party Headquarters uphold justice and quickly find a solution to avoid the expansion of disputes. Wu promised to consult with the Municipal Government and then determine a solution, but hoped that the workers would fight in an orderly manner to avoid causing other disputes. They all left after 1:00 PM.

(Appealing for Assistance) In addition to sending representatives to petition, the Fifth District Cigarette Workers' Union also submitted a petition to the party and government for assistance. The original petition stated: "Submitted for the matter of petitioning. The British American Tobacco Company suddenly closed the first factory in Pudong on the 12th of this month without reason, and more than 3,000 workers in the entire factory were suddenly plunged into despair. It is unbearable to speak of the sadness and fear. Looking back, the first factory has been in operation for more than 30 years and is the ancestor of the company's factories in China, earning profits of no less than tens of millions, all of which are the crystallization of our workers' blood and sweat. In recent years, the company's management has been unable to unify, often causing disputes. The workers are deeply aware that the country is in a difficult situation and have made concessions step by step, but the company has taken advantage of the opportunity to gain an inch. In the middle of last month, the factory used the excuse of sluggish business to continuously reduce work. After the Municipal Government's approval number 30 ordered compliance, the factory was not allowed to reduce working hours without submitting a request to the主管官署 for approval. Unexpectedly, the factory refused to comply. On the 10th of this month, it again arbitrarily reduced the working hours, only doing 36 hours per week. The union believed that it was difficult to maintain the workers' livelihood and petitioned the party and government agencies. We also received the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau's approval number 3614, ordering the factory to postpone implementation temporarily in order to provide some security for the lives of 7,000 workers. Unexpectedly, on the 12th of this month, the company regarded the orders of the Municipal Government and the Social Affairs Bureau as worthless, using the excuse of sluggish business and refusing to follow orders, and actually closed the old factory, plunging more than 3,000 workers in the entire factory into despair and causing panic in the society. The previous reduction in work was due to the use of new high-speed machines to increase speed, and the outsourcing of raw material rolling to factories such as Citibank, resulting in overproduction, which has nothing to do with sluggish business. The closure of the first factory this time is because some workers have been working for two or three years and their wages are all above one or two yuan. The intention is to lay off old workers and save wages, and then hire new workers when the factory resumes operation in the future. If this example is set, not only will British American Tobacco's factories in China follow suit, but other factories will also follow suit, affecting the future of workers across the country, which is no small matter. In this crisis, our hearts are filled with anxiety. We are sending another group of 39 representatives, including Chen Peide, Lou Jingguan, and Zhang Ziping, to come forward to petition and present everything in person, hoping that you will provide a solution for us to follow."

(Forming a Strike Committee) In order to seek the immediate resumption of work at the old British American Tobacco Company factory, the workers of the new and old factories resolved at the representatives' meeting the day before yesterday to organize a factory resumption movement committee, and decided that if there was still no solution before Thursday of this week, it would be changed to a strike committee. Now that the deadline is approaching and the factory still has no hope of resuming work, the Fifth District Cigarette Workers' Union decided to hold a workers' representative meeting at the Lannidu clubhouse at 5:00 PM today to discuss the formation of a strike committee.

As the assistant manager, he disregarded the legal interests of the plaintiffs' shareholders, intending to illegally possess the factory invested in by the plaintiffs that he managed for himself or a third party, and for the benefit of himself or a third party in handling the plaintiffs' affairs, he engaged in an illegal transfer that violated his duties. This is a crime in violation of Articles 357 and 366 of the Criminal Law. The court accepted the complaint and opened the trial yesterday. After the plaintiff stated the intention of the lawsuit, the defendant denied everything. The court immediately ordered the start of the debate and announced the conclusion of the trial, scheduling sentencing for the 26th of this month.

A Child with Two Heads: One Head Asleep, One Head Awake 177

Yi Xiangshan, a native of Hubei, recently acquired a strange child. The child has two heads at both ends, with four hands and three feet. The lower part is fused together, resembling twins who have not been fully developed and separated. It has been a year since it was born, and it is fed with milk. Its crying and laughing are no different from ordinary children, except that sometimes one head is asleep while the other is still awake. A few days ago, Yi brought the strange child to the home of a relative, Liu Shunfa Rice Shop, at No. 14 Wujianong, Pudong, for a temporary stay. Unexpectedly, nearby residents, who had never heard of a two-headed child, could not help but regard it as a strange thing and flocked to the rice shop to watch. Yi, seeing that it was a rare commodity, stayed at the Pudong Hospital to avoid the crowds. The Yangjing District Tongcai Charity Association learned of the matter and, with Yi's consent, began selling tickets for public viewing in a building at a certain number on Dongchang Road yesterday. The proceeds from the tickets were used to fund the association. The audience was quite crowded.

Someone Reveals That Buddhist Monks Went to Japan to Participate in a Humiliating National Conference; Buddhist Association Expresses Surprise and Will Schedule a Meeting to Discuss 180

According to Datong News Agency, the day before yesterday evening, a kind of anonymous mailed letter was found in this city. After carefully checking the postmark of the mailing location on the envelope, it belonged to Nanjing. Pile Driving Collapses Neighboring House; Ancient Tomb Discovered Underground 192

The houses in Lianyuanli, Mubiao Street, Fangbang Road in the city belong to several surnames. The northeast side was renovated the year before last. The southwest side belongs to the Wu, Lu, and other surnames. Recently, because the Wu surname sold the property to the Lin surname from Beiping, it was rebuilt into a three-story steel-concrete residential building, which was contracted by Qiasun Construction Factory. There was a contract with a deadline for completion. Therefore, ditching and pile driving have been underway in recent days to make three-in-one soil foundations. Because the neighboring Lu surname's lean-to was not supported beforehand, the foundation of the wall shook and collapsed. One or two lean-tos were destroyed. Fortunately, it was daytime and no one was injured. The injured Lu surname owner reported it to the responsible public security bureau of the first sub-district, who sent personnel to the scene to investigate. It was found that the Qiasun Construction Factory had reduced the work in various ways, which caused the collapse. Moreover, there were several ancient tombs underground, all built of brick corridors, which were extremely strong. Two of the ancient tombs happened to be located at the ditching and pile driving site and had been opened. However, the coffins had rotted, leaving only skeletons. The skeletons were bright red in color. Because there was water in the corridor, they were all picked up from the water. There were also small items such as ancient coins and jade objects, which were all hidden by the workers. Although the tomb had brick boards, they had been broken and the inscriptions were difficult to identify. It is not known whose family tomb it is, and no one has claimed the bones. There are still two tombs left underground, which have not been excavated or reburied. It is said that the Lu surname is now demanding that work be stopped pending resolution.

Tragic Murder Case Beside Zhaofeng Garden: Immoral Woman with Other Desires Plots with New Lover to Kill Old Flame 193

Around 11 PM the night before last, a love triangle murder case occurred beside the small stone bridge near Zhaofeng Garden, next to the Shanghai West Caojiadu Extra-Settlement Road YMCA. The deceased was named Qiang Fugen. The adulterous lover and the female lead have both fled without a trace. The detailed circumstances are investigated and recorded below:

(Shouts for Help Resound) At 11 PM the night before last, Gao Shanxian, a policeman from the Sixth District of Shanghai West Extra-Settlement Road, received a report from a Wang surname resident of the YMCA compound, stating that a man had been assassinated near the small stone bridge and was lying on the ground. Two Western men and women happened to pass by, heard the sound, and caught a glimpse, instructing the resident to report the incident. The policeman immediately went to the location and found blood everywhere, indicating severe injuries. He hired a car to take the injured man back to the district.

(Death Due to Severe Injuries) The injured man was still conscious when he arrived at the district. After being questioned by District Chief Tan and District Officer Xing, he was immediately sent to the Red Cross Hospital on Haige Road for treatment. Doctors found a knife wound about two to three inches deep in his waist and abdomen. His internal organs were damaged, and he lost too much blood. Despite emergency surgery, his injuries were too severe, and he died at 0:50 AM yesterday.

(Love Quadrangle) According to the deceased's statement, his name was Qiang Fugen, 30 years old, from Wuxi, currently residing at No. 3 Yikang Lane, Huajin Lane, Sanma Road, Public Concession. He had no family in Shanghai. He used to work as a clerk at the Shanghai Telephone Company and later as a cashier at a dance hall. He became unemployed in January of this year. Four years ago, he became acquainted with Mrs. Lu Wang, the wife of Lu Zixi (also known as Lu Yizhang), residing at No. 1 Tongqing Lane, Minguo Road. They were deeply in love and often met secretly in hotels. Unexpectedly, in January of this year, the woman became secretly involved with Zhang Hanzhang, who runs a butcher shop at No. 6 Huikang Lane, Caojiadu, Shanghai West. She became tired of the old and favored the new, developing a dislike for Qiang and colluding with Zhang to plot his murder.

(Luring for Murder) The day before yesterday afternoon, the woman tricked Qiang to Shanghai West, feigning intimacy. They went to Zhaofeng Garden to play. Around 10 PM, they left the garden and walked to the small stone bridge at Sujiajiao. Unexpectedly, her new lover, Zhang Hanzhang, had been lying in wait there. Seeing Qiang approaching, he grabbed him and pulled out a sharp dagger from his waist, stabbing Qiang violently in the right abdomen three times. Qiang fell to the ground in extreme pain. Zhang and the woman, seeing that their goal had been achieved, fled out of the alley, each hiring a rickshaw for two small silver coins to get to Wujiaochang, where they got off and hired a Haining Company car to escape Shanghai.

(Separate Investigations) The rickshaw puller, seeing that the man and woman looked panicked and suspicious, reported to the local police post. When the police arrived after receiving the report, the car had already gone far away. The police took the rickshaw puller, named Ju Jinhui, to the district. District Chief Tan immediately dispatched Patrol Officer Cheng, along with Detective Team Leader Wu Kezhong, Detectives Yang Qing, Wang Yixin, etc., to No. 1 Tongqing Lane, Minguo Road, to arrest Lu Zixi, the female lead's husband, and bring him back to the district. Patrol Officer Long was also dispatched with bailiffs to No. 6 Huikang Lane to arrest Zhang Hanzhang's wife, Mrs. Zhang Wang (32 years old), and concubine, Zhang Cai (22 years old), and bring them to the district as well.

(Seizing the Murder Weapon) Yesterday morning, Patrol Officers Cheng and Long went to the scene of the incident to investigate. They found a sharp knife about eight to nine inches long in the nearby grass. After bringing it back to the district, they ordered the local Baotou to report it to the local court for examination. Subsequently, the court appointed a prosecutor to inspect the scene and confirm that the deceased had been fatally stabbed. The Baotou was instructed to prepare a coffin for burial. District Chief Tan then questioned Lu Zixi, Mrs. Zhang Wang, and Zhang Cai separately, deciding to temporarily detain them pending further investigation. The rickshaw puller was released.

Chen Zhongxing, a Cantonese overseas Chinese residing in the upstairs of No. 2 Wufeng Lane at the intersection of Xiafei Road and Luban Road in the French Concession, was previously friendly with his fellow townsman Tan Lengyu. After being released from prison in early spring of this year, he invited Qian Qichang, a Zhenjiang native and fellow inmate, to rent the main hall upstairs at No. 28 Baoren Lane, Xiafei Road. On the morning of March 27, at about 8 AM, Tan lured Chen to No. 28 Baoren Lane, first ordering him to play chess with Chen to pass the time. At about 1 PM, Tan made his move to kill Chen, hitting him on the head with a cloth-wrapped iron hammer, causing him to be injured and die instantly. Qian fled first. Tan then wrapped the body in bedding and clothes, sprinkled kerosene on it, and set it on fire, attempting to destroy the body and eliminate evidence. After setting the fire, he calmly escaped. Qian was sent to the Second Special Court and prosecuted for premeditated murder under Article 284 of the Criminal Code. Detective Superintendent Jin and others rushed to Guangzhou to arrest Tan, but were unsuccessful. The details of Qian's trial have been reported previously. The court appointed a pro bono lawyer to defend Qian, and the trial concluded. Yesterday morning, on the date of sentencing, the police brought Qian to the court. At 10:30 AM, Judge Xiong Huiping presided over the First Criminal Court and sentenced Qian Qichang to fourteen years of imprisonment for assisting in premeditated murder. The number of days of pre-trial detention was converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. During the appeal period, he will be detained in the detention center pending further instructions.

Reading News

Galileo's Experiments and Newton's Law of Universal Gravitation 199

Reading Guidance:

Recently, I have been at home away from school and studying all subjects on my own, so I always encounter difficulties! I was reading physics and had questions that left me full of doubts. I was delighted to learn that your newspaper has a reading guidance column to answer readers' questions, so I am writing to ask for help with the following pressing questions: All students of physics are familiar with Galileo's Leaning Tower of Pisa experiment and Newton's Law of Universal Gravitation. My questions arise from these. According to Galileo's experiment, when objects are not hindered by air resistance, they fall freely from the same height at the same time and reach the ground at the same time, regardless of their size or weight. Newton's Law states that the gravitational force between objects is directly proportional to the product of their masses. It seems that these two principles are contradictory. I would like to present a few points for discussion. I do not dare to question the wisdom of the ancients, but I am genuinely puzzled.

1. According to Galileo, objects fall at the same speed if they are not resisted or subject to friction. This is true in terms of area and speed, but with mass, it seems to contradict Newton's Law of Universal Gravitation, which states that "the magnitude of the gravitational force is directly proportional to the mass…"

2. Suppose that objects in a vacuum have nothing to do with gravity and are not affected by the earth's gravity. If this is true, then objects in a vacuum cannot move and should remain stationary in space because energy cannot be created. Since they are not subject to any gravitational or motive force, how can they move and fall? Therefore, this principle cannot be true.

3. If it is said that the molecules that make up an object are constantly in motion rather than static, so energy already exists in the object and does not need to be supplied. The reason why objects are usually still is because of the earth's gravity. Once the constraints from all sides are released, the potential energy will be manifested as motion. However, if the object is not subject to the influence of gravity and moves by the potential energy of the molecules, then its direction of motion is not fixed. Why, as in Galileo's vacuum experiment, is there only downward motion, and no motion upward, to the left, or to the right? The fact that it still has a tendency to move toward the earth is clear proof that it is still related to the earth's gravity.

In conclusion, I believe that the theories of the two masters are contradictory. However, I have little knowledge and cannot determine what is wrong. I lack the means of explanation and have no equipment for practical research. But I am consumed by a desire for knowledge, so I boldly ask

Your esteemed selves to provide me with an antidote to my doubts. I would be eternally grateful.

(Letter from Qu Qihuai, Yuanling)

"If there is no air resistance, objects of different masses must fall at the same acceleration." This law was discovered by Galileo and completely proven by Newton and Bessel. We can use the Law of Universal Gravitation to prove this law, which shows that these two laws are not mutually contradictory. According to the Law of Universal Gravitation: The gravitational force between two objects is directly proportional to the product of the masses of the two objects and inversely proportional to the square of the distance between the two objects. That is:

E = Gmm/r^2 (C is the gravitational constant)

Now suppose there are three objects with masses m1, m2, and m3.

These three objects are in the same place in the air, at an equal distance r from the earth. Suppose the mass of the earth is M, then the gravitational force between these three objects and the earth must be:

FI = GMmI/r^2 F-2 = G-Mm2 F3 = GMm3/r^2

According to Newton's Second Law: Force is the product of mass and acceleration. It can be deduced that:

A (Acceleration) = F (Force)/m (Mass)

Then the acceleration of the above three objects should be:

AI=EI/mIGMI2A2=F2m2GM-2

A3 = F3-Am3 = GM-r3

That is: AI = A2 = 3 = G I-r2

It is proven that: objects fall freely from the same place in the air at the same time. If there is no air or other resistance, they must fall to the ground at the same time, regardless of the mass of the objects.

(Another proof) We already know: force is the product of mass and acceleration, that is, F = ma.

Then: FI = mia.

Already know: FI = GMmI-r2

Then: mTa = GMmI-r2

That is a = GM-r2

Using the same method to calculate F2 and F3, the same result is obtained.

If you can understand these proofs, your first question will be resolved, and your second and third questions will be answered without question.

(This letter was answered by Mr. Ding Guizhong, a natural science expert specially appointed by this department.)

He also asked the company for three days of leave. He found a spare house at No. 49 Yongji Lane, Xinzha Road, and moved in the day before yesterday. Yesterday, his mother-in-law and others wanted to return to their hometown, so he sent his mother-in-law to the station in the morning. After getting on the train, he went home. He wanted to find his uniform and hat in the company's box to prepare for work. Suddenly, he found a photo of his wife in the box. He asked Yu because she usually didn't have photos, and even if she took photos, there should be two. Where did the other one go? She couldn't answer, and then claimed that she had given it to a young sister, and

roared loudly at me 205

deliberately provoking a quarrel. He didn't want to argue with her, so he left in anger and went to the company to do business. But he thought that Yu was already restless and usually spent 70 to 80 yuan of his hard-earned wages at will, with unknown purposes. He was very angry and had no intention of doing business, so he continued to take two days of leave from the company and went home immediately. Unexpectedly, when he entered the door, he saw his wife and Gao lying on the bed, talking intimately. He couldn't help but feel angry and loudly asked Gao why he had come again. Because he was afraid of him, he moved here. As he spoke, he slapped his wife twice. Gao, seeing his lover being humiliated, looked around and

took a pig-killing knife 206

from the door, intending to strike. At this time, he was outnumbered and afraid of danger. If he didn't take precautions, he would be harmed. So he bravely stepped forward, snatched the knife, and seeing his wife willing to be cheap, he stabbed his wife's leg with the knife. The deceased Gao Yihe stepped forward to help and wanted to snatch the kitchen knife back, accidentally injuring his left leg fatally. Qin also hired Attorney Chen Tingrui to defend him. Judge Feng Shide verified the confession and ordered the defendant Qin A'fa to be remanded in custody and adjourned for seven days for another hearing. The detectives then took Qin down and escorted him to the mortuary. Prosecutor Diao Chengtang, along with clerk Wang Zuyi and medical examiners Wei and Zhang, arrived at the mortuary to examine the body. After a thorough examination, they took their seats and questioned Qin A'fa again. They stated that the examination revealed that the deceased Gao Yihe was indeed stabbed in the leg by Qin A'fa before his death. The body was handed over to Pulun Mountain Villa for burial.

Spring and Autumn

A Record of Lingering Fragrance 207

— Originally written by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Besides these, like hand towels, powder, rouge, combs, etc., everything a female emperor uses for makeup is available. The most ingenious is this box, which can be used as a handrail when lowered and instantly turns into a long mirror when lifted: thus, the Empress Dowager can dress up as much as she likes on the way without being seen by others.

She absolutely did not allow her people to steal a peek at her, so no one dared to stand and watch when her imperial carriage passed by on the street. In fact, we all knew that those commoners often poked small holes in the paper windows to secretly watch the imperial carriage passing in front of their doors: the only one who didn't know was the Empress Dowager herself. Even if someone told her, she would not believe that there were people so daring. However, in order to ensure extra secrecy, special curtains were hung on both sides of the window of this imperial carriage. Two curtains were hung on each side of the window, the same length. However, the one closer to the inside, two in total on the left and right - because it was right next to where she was sitting - was made of yellow satin lined with silk wadding. Not only could people outside not see in, but she herself could not see out; wouldn't this be too stuffy? So the one on the outside (there were two in total on the left and right) was changed to transparent light gauze, so that she could vaguely see the scenery outside without being seen by people outside. If she still felt that it was too unclear or too difficult to see through this layer of light gauze, she could lean forward, gently pull open some of the gauze curtains, and look sideways. Even so, outsiders need not think of spying on her. Even the sharpest eyes could only see a few of her fingers at most. (40)

Bright Moon 208

— Fu Yizhi

A boundless azure sky, hanging a round mirror-like bright moon, sparkling and clear, without a trace of dust, vaguely like an unparalleled beauty in the instant after bathing, stark naked, craning her neck to look out the window; sometimes, those light wisp-like clouds, pushed by the gentle breeze to her bosom, enveloping her, but that is just like a layer of light gauze draped over icy skin and jade flesh, not detracting from her beauty, but rather adding to her charm, I am truly fascinated by her, because she is so beautiful. When I was in my hometown, I would often run alone to the lawn, sit on the ground, and look up, watching her being covered by dense clouds and mist, and I would feel sorry for her, watching her jump out of the clouds lively, and I would be indescribably happy, she pondered, and I pondered, and I and she had merged into a spiritual communion, the cold wind tousled my hair, and the dew dampened my clothes, I did not care; people said I was crazy, I just laughed it off, because this beautiful, purified state of mind, can only be told to those who understand, and is really difficult to tell to others. When I return extremely tired, the moon teaches me to walk with my shadow as a companion; I take off my clothes and go to bed, and the moon secretly climbs into the window lattice again, moves onto the bed, kisses me, caresses me, until I fall asleep, that round face of hers, always radiates a benevolent light, when I was in my hometown, she was like this, when I am away from home, she is also like this; if the sun symbolizes a father who combines grace and power, she is a mother who nourishes us with pure love.

However, even a small flame can be obscured by many flames, on the road flanked by tall buildings, in the alleys, she is often robbed of her place by the incandescent electric light, if not for "a full moon tonight", I would have forgotten her long ago, this is my fault.

Paper House 209

— Zui Chi Sheng

"Look, everyone, go to 'Shenxiang Pavilion' to see the burning paper houses." People, big and small, who like to join in the fun in the alleys, were shouting like this. This large, × residence was holding a Buddhist service in Shenxiang Pavilion. There were quite a few male and female guests. Added to the people outside coming to see the excitement, it was extremely crowded for a while. At this time, several workers were putting branches, straw, and the like in the open space in the courtyard. On top, they spread reed mats flat. Then they moved the already made paper house from the main hall and hooked it up one after another. There was a front yard, and a back yard. In addition to the halls and厢房, there were kitchens and garages. It was truly magnificent: all kinds of furnishings were prepared inside, such as wireless radios and other entertainment items, everything was available, just like the real thing. Although it was a miniature paper house, people could actually go in and out. Inside, there were also piles of underworld money and paper ingots, so it could be considered that everything for enjoyment was already there.

So the audience all praised and said, "Although the old lady is dead, she is really blessed, she can still live in such an elaborate house." Some people also sighed and said, "I heard that this paper house cost more than one hundred and several tens of yuan in silver when it was ordered from the paper goods store. That's almost half a year's worth of food for a poor family!"

After the monks finished chanting sutras: they lit a fire and burned the paper house. Suddenly, the flames soared, with a burst of crackling sounds. In an instant, this "reverent in appearance" paper house turned to ashes.

At this time, the family members and relatives and friends of the × residence all had smiles on their faces. It seemed that by doing this, they had fulfilled the "rites of a son". The deceased old lady, under the nine springs, could get some comfort.

Northeast Fourth Company Commander 210

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-ninth Reply Letter With Sadness, Claiming Solitude, Listen Together To Swear Blood To Dismantle Jingzhong

Jiang said: If you want to write a reply, that's fine, but after you write the letter, you must read it to me. If it's not right, I can tell you to change it. Don't think I don't recognize the words, I have eaten a few more pounds of salt than you, and maybe I can see things you can't see. Guizhi said: That's fine too. Originally, I couldn't recognize even three words, so what's the point of writing a letter. But I can't ask anyone to write this kind of letter, so I have to make do with it myself. After saying that, he immediately took the letter to his own room, closed the door, and slowly started writing. After writing for about two hours, looking up the thousand-character classic and elementary school textbooks, he pieced together a letter. Then he ordered someone to take the letter to the front yard to report to Jiang. When Jiang saw Guizhi ordering someone to bring the letter in, he knew that he was going to read it to him, so he grabbed Guizhi's sleeve and pulled him straight into the inner room, then let him sit on the edge of the brick bed, sat down opposite him, and asked him softly? Read it, don't shout. So Guizhi held the letter and read:

To Uncle Ji Zhi: I was very surprised to receive your letter. I am now on very good terms with Company Commander Zhao, as everyone knows. As the saying goes, a horse should not be saddled twice, and a woman should not marry two men. Although I am the daughter of a poor family, I also know some propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame. How can there be a virtuous wife who communicates with others. Since you have written a letter, I can't stop you, I hope you won't do this in the future, if people find out, it would be a joke. You are a gentleman, do I need to say more? Gleanings on Baoshan Road 211

— Yan

Baoshan Road north crosses Qiujiang Road, less than two hundred paces, and Hongxing Road comes from the northwest to meet. Currently, at the intersection of these two roads, the Shanghai Police Memorial Tower is being built. Construction has been underway for several months, with dozens of stonemasons chiseling away day and night. The tower base is built into a trapezoid shape, wider at the back and narrower at the front, according to the terrain, all made of stone. There are three stone steps on the front and back to climb up, with giant stones used as railings, also divided into three levels, getting higher and higher towards the back. A stone statue platform is paved in the middle, and a square stone the size of an eight immortals table is used as the base in the center, with a tower core more than ten feet high glued on with cement. The tower core will be surrounded by giant stones measuring a foot thick, five feet wide, and ten feet long to form a square pillar shape. Currently, these four giant stones have been chiseled out. On one stone is carved the inscription "Shanghai Municipal Martyrs' Police Memorial Tower" in twelve large characters, inscribed by Mayor Wu Tiecheng, and it has also been engraved. The unveiling ceremony can be held soon when these four giant stones are erected. After the January 28th Incident, Baoshan Road was covered in scars, but now it has been slightly rebuilt. The addition of this solemn and magnificent memorial tower is enough to add to its embellishment.

On the side of Baoshan Road, there are open spaces everywhere. The former Chinese mansions are now flat ground. Since the beginning of spring, the survivors of the disaster have greatly developed the interest in flying kites. On days when the wind is gentle and the sun is warm, they all come to this open space to launch a kite into the sky. On the ground, the young and old are bustling, looking up and laughing. In the sky, there are centipedes, eagles, four-cornered and eight-cornered kites, long snakes, airplanes, and other kites in various shapes, nothing is too strange.

Sometimes moving, sometimes still, sometimes sinking, sometimes floating, each taking advantage of the long wind to compete. The once densely populated Baoshan Road has now transformed into a place for chasing kites. Who could have foreseen this two and a half years ago?

Character Sketches

Random Notes from Yu Kan 212

Qian Da of Jiangnan

In the late Qing Dynasty, there were many writers who followed Zong Ding, and the trend of the times made it extremely popular for a while, precisely because Dragon's writing was unrestrained and bold, with a wonderfulness that could not be measured. At that time, Tiannan Dun Sou's great name shook Hainan, Dun Sou had entered the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom, not only was his writing strangely unrestrained, but he was also clear about the general trend of the world, and the strategy of war and defense. The scholars of the southeast all regarded him as the head of the literati, but his school of thought originated from Ding. Zou Jiugai, Mr. Zou Jiugai of my county, had been with Dun Sou for the longest time, and deeply inherited his mantle. His writing could melt the old and new of that time in five furnaces, and his poems and lyrics were also deeply affectionate and meaningful, not to be seen as ordinary chapters of singing about the wind and admiring the moon. Mr. had been famous at home and abroad for his poems and essays between Tongzhi and Guangxu, and enjoyed a literary name for thirty years, which can be said to be a long time. In the twelfth year of the Republic of China, I and my old friend Jin Shishou met Mr. at the Shousi Lou in Xujiahui, Shanghai. I was just a young man and Mr. was already over seventy. We felt like old acquaintances at first sight and talked for half a day. We then made a friendship that transcended age. At that time, I wrote six poems to record the event, which are published in Free Talk. Mr. broke his foot while traveling, and I often went to visit him in my spare time. Later, Mr. moved back to his hometown of Houzhai, and I never saw him again, only occasionally exchanging letters. In the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, I and Cheng Xiaoqing, Xu Bibo and other gentlemen founded the Gongyuan Cinema in Wumen. Mr. read the newspaper and learned about it and sent a letter to congratulate us. One morning, I was still asleep, when Mr. Zhou came from Xiyou Su, drove to visit. The servants, seeing that I had not gotten up and that Mr.'s clothes were not fancy and he had a limp, were arrogant and impolite, and refused to let him in. Mr. then threw his card and left. When I got up, the servant brought in the card, saying that a lame old man had come a moment ago, told him that Mr. had not gotten up, and left. Looking at the card, it was Mr.'s name. I blamed the servant for being rude and thinking that the world judged people by their clothes. If Mr. had worn fancy clothes, the servant would have been respectful and called me to wake up. There is a saying that dogs look down on people, and there are many people with dog eyes in the world, let alone servants? What's the point of blaming him? I quickly hired a rickshaw to visit him. At that time, Mr. was living in a Buddhist temple. We were happy to see each other and talk about the past. However, Mr. had already shown signs of decline and was no longer as robust as he used to be, which made me feel sad for a long time. A few years later, Mr. died. I never thought that this hurried meeting would be our last. Mr. was a lyricist of a generation, but his life after death was very desolate. It is a pity that heaven gave talent to people like this!

To see the true picture of officialdom, there is no better book than Mr. Nanting Tingchang's "Records of the True Appearance of Officialdom", which can be said to be colorful and vividly depicts the ugliness. It is said that in the mountains, the spring water is clear, but it becomes turbid when it comes out of the mountains. The environment makes it so. I have seen many people over the years, but no one is more honest and treats people with kindness than Mr. Wu Zonglian of Yucheng. Mr. Wu Zonglian's courtesy name is Yiqing. He served in important positions during the late Qing Dynasty. After the Republic of China, he served as a member of the National Assembly and ministers to various countries. He was especially proficient in French and was a veteran of our country's diplomatic circles. Today, among the important figures of the party and the country, there are not a few who have studied under him. When I met Mr., he was the director of the French Concession Public Works Bureau. He was already over seventy years old. At first sight, I knew that he was a kind and amiable elder. At that time, Mr. also served as the general manager of a certain shipping company. He was not familiar with this field, but a few people used his name for other purposes. I learned the details and strongly advised him not to sacrifice his reputation for nothing. Later, Mr. also realized this and resolutely left. However, because of his honest nature, he was easily fooled by others everywhere. Often, before one thing was finished, he would fall into the trap again in an instant. He had to make compensation because he guaranteed for others, and he had been involved in lawsuits for a long time, but he still failed in the end. However, he suffered a lot of losses in terms of reputation because he was played by villains several times. After his death, some people said that he was too eager to seek advancement and was too persistent in one thing, to the point where he was scolded in person. I alone said that this was actually forced by the environment. At that time, Mr. had to bear a burden of five or six hundred gold per month. In recent years, his later years had been gradually declining, his income had been sharply reduced, and he had to borrow money to make a living. He found it really difficult not to seek a way out. It was pitiful that he was still running around in his old age. However, summing up his life, he was too honest and not smart enough. Therefore, he went through officialdom, but he still had nothing to his name and died unhappily. However, it is rare and valuable to be an official without money in today's world. Mr. once asked me to introduce him to the Kuomintang. Unexpectedly, Mr. had already passed away as soon as the central party certificate was issued. This certificate is still with me.

Philippine Newspapers Uphold Justice and Criticize the Philippine Sports Authorities A Country That Is Not Yet Independent Dares to Publicly Violate World Opinion Arrogantly Wants to Recognize the Pseudo-Organization Cowardly, Untrustworthy, and Without Independent Personality 213

This is extremely arrogant. The Philippine sports community has also launched a great resistance to the reckless actions of a few leaders who violate public opinion, and they are unwilling to join the new association. Japan filed an unreasonable protest. The Mermaid Alarmed the Philippine Island 220

Our Dao Da Zhonghua's mermaid is really a mermaid. When she swam from Hong Kong to the President McKinley, she stirred up the air on the wheel. Look at her bare legs, changing three or four sets of clothes as light as cicada wings a day, swimming east to west, west to east. The athletes' eyes were really dazzled by her swimming. Now our Dao mermaid has swam to the Philippines again, and the hot air in Manila has been stirred up again. The dormitories of the Philippine Women's University are crowded with journalists and overseas Chinese every day. The newspapers publish her photos in different poses every day. No matter where she goes, whoever she meets, when they talk about Chinese athletes, they talk about the mermaid. So "China produces beauties" and "China produces mermaids" spread throughout the Philippine Islands. Our mermaid is really a mermaid, but we hope that our mermaid will not only focus on the word "beauty", but forget that she is a swimming fish.

The General Life of Athletes 221

Our delegation, except for General Team Wang Zhengting and his wife, who live in the home of Consul General Kuang Guanglin, and the two representatives Hao Gengsheng and Shen Siliang, who live in the Manila Hotel, the female athletes live in the Philippine Women's University, and the male athletes live in Lacha University. They are all very close to the Rizal Sports Ground (Japanese and Dutch Indian athletes also live here). The dormitory is the original classroom, and the congressmen and athletes are the same. Twenty or thirty people are crammed into one room. Except for a small bed and a small mosquito net, there is nothing else. Everyone is living a very simple life happily. Philippine mosquitoes are really good. Every morning when we wake up from a tired sleep, we always find many red bumps on our bodies. However, after a day of fatigue, when we fall on the bed, we are like dead people, letting the mosquitoes suck some blood. We really don't care about it, so we don't think it's hard. The food is contracted to a Cantonese overseas Chinese chef. On the first day, we ate Chinese food, a few dishes that were not sweet, not salty, not sour, not spicy. Although we were hungry, we still found it difficult to swallow. The next day, we changed to Western food, but it was just him serving the same dishes again. However, our funds are insufficient, and we cannot bring more than a dozen chefs with us like the Japanese. There is no way to do it. The athletes have all made up their minds to fill their stomachs as long as they go to the dining hall, and they must fight hard on the sports field. Therefore, everything is calm and quiet, and there is no war in the dining hall.

The Weather Is Extremely Hot and the Practice Is Hard 222

The weather in May is the hottest time in the Philippine Islands. Schools are on summer vacation, and the mercury in the thermometer often rises to one hundred degrees. For the sake of our athletes, especially those from the north, it is really a bit unbearable to practice non-stop in such a climate. They sweat all day long, and everyone is not afraid of the stench, and there is a layer of black oil on their faces. Everyone thinks that it has increased their healthy beauty, but their skin is tanned and scorched, even to the point of cracking. Everyone is gritting their teeth, which is really a bit difficult to endure. They take cold showers every day, and the bodies that are drenched in sweat are poured over their heads with cold water. If it weren't for the fact that they would sweat again after washing, I don't believe that everyone could safely maintain their health.

The Reporter Was Actually Surrounded 223

Journalists from various countries who came specifically to explore news about the conference, Japan came a total of sixteen, but our country is just a small area. Compared in quantity, it is really like a small witch seeing a big witch. But there is one thing that can comfort everyone, that is, the small area did not lose the face of the country because of the small number. On the first day of arrival, as soon as I walked into the dormitory, I was surrounded by a large number of colleagues from the local Chinese and Western newspapers. The next day's newspapers, in addition to the written records, also published a photo of the small area in an important section. This really made me a little flattered. At 7:30 p.m. on the 10th, the Manila Journalists Association hosted a banquet for foreign journalists at the largest and largest St. Anne's Dance Hall in the world. Important local colleagues personally came to receive us. In addition to attending on time, I also invited Shi Zhaokang and Zhou Jiaqi, who were also sending telegrams for Shen Xin, and representative Hao Gengsheng to go with me. However, a large number of Japanese colleagues did not come until after 8:30 p.m. In the initial impression, we had already won a small victory. In the middle of the banquet, the host and guests inevitably gave speeches to each other. The host was the Associated Press's Moore and the Philippine Free Society's Rogets, who delivered welcome speeches. We pushed Mr. Hao to deliver a reply speech, and his eloquent remarks won a lot of applause. The Japanese representative stood up, said a few incoherent words simply, and sat down. The banquet ended after several special dance performances. A large number of Japanese reporters left silently and without beginning or end. We went around for a while before saying goodbye. At this solemn and grand colleague banquet, we finally did not disgrace our mission and won a little face for the country.

It is reported that the competition will conclude on the 27th, at which point the champions of each group will be determined. The Groveling Philippine Sophora Japonica 228

Yesterday, we detailed the illegal dissolution of the Far Eastern Athletic Association by Japan and the Philippines and the subsequent organization of the so-called East Asian Amateur Athletic Association. Relying on its political and diplomatic threats, Japan compelled the Philippine representative to accept orders from another power, leaving them no choice but to succumb. As a result, our country, which has always been at the mercy of others, has also suffered a setback in sports diplomacy today, influenced by the decline of our national vitality. However, the sudden change in the Philippine representative's attitude warrants further examination.

The Philippines prepared for this year's Far Eastern Championship Games for over a year, spending more than a million yuan on projects such as building the Rizal Memorial Stadium. During this time of economic panic, in addition to making every effort to make up the cost, they also had to rely on ticket sales to supplement the expenses. However, after Japan proposed the requirement for the participation of the puppet organization, during the trilateral roundtable conference convened in Shanghai, the Philippine representative strictly maintained neutrality, refraining from expressing any opinions, fearing any disadvantage to either China or Japan, which might hinder the Games from proceeding as scheduled and cause significant economic losses. Therefore, they tried their best to appease both China and Japan, hoping to preserve the Philippines' position and the painstaking effort of investing heavily in the 10th Games, so that the Games could be held as scheduled. Thus, they proposed submitting this issue to the regular executive committee meeting to be held during the Games, and the roundtable conference temporarily ended as such. Our country fell into their trap.

As a result, the Games were able to proceed as scheduled. The overseas Chinese in the Philippines believed that the Philippine representative's unchanging attitude at the Shanghai roundtable conference and the failure of Japan's cunning schemes were fortunate and offered their full spiritual and material support to the Philippine Athletic Association, welcoming the motherland on one hand and supporting the Philippines on the other. The Games proceeded smoothly, and ticket sales increased significantly. The Philippine Athletic Association itself should have expressed sincere friendship in terms of moral and spiritual values, given our Athletic Association's sincere maintenance and the overseas Chinese's wholehearted assistance. Unexpectedly, not only did they not do this, but they also drastically changed their sinister faces, believing that their goal had been achieved. They intensified their efforts to assist the wicked, colluding with Japanese imperialists to dissolve the Far Eastern Athletic Association through extraordinary means and initiate the pseudo-organization of the East Asian Athletic Association. People like the Filipinos are worse than snakes and scorpions; it is not enough to talk about eating their flesh and sucking their blood to vent our indignation.

Second Day of the Middle School Athletic Association Volleyball Tournament 237

Minli Has Already Won the Women's Championship

The second day of the Middle School Athletic Association Volleyball Tournament was held yesterday. A gentle breeze and thin clouds made for pleasant conditions. Each of the athletes was energetic and competed fiercely on the track and field. In the first match, Fudan Brothers fought against each other in their own camp. Fudan Middle was no match for Fudan Practical, losing by two to one. However, both sides fought earnestly during the battle and did not show favoritism, so the scores were very close. Hujiang defeated Minli, like a tiger capturing a sheep. Jinan defeated Fudan Practical, expending all their strength. The Fudan Practical team had many veteran players, and Fudan has a tradition of producing volleyball stars. However, their defeat to Jinan yesterday was purely due to panic in the heat of the moment. In addition, Jinan's front-row blocking was strong. Although Fudan Practical tried their best to block, it was difficult to be effective. But Fudan Practical's defeat means that the final will become a multi-faceted love affair. If Jinan can defeat Hujiang again today, they can win the Group 中 final. If they are defeated by Hujiang again, they will form a three-legged situation with Fudan Practical and Hujiang, and they will have to fight again. And the battle between Guanghua and ? scheduled for today will have to wait for a good time. On the women's side, Minli did not have to use an arrow or spill blood when they first met Patriotic, and they got two points easily. Yesterday, they defeated Guanghua again, making it easy. The championship is securely won, and there is no problem. Today's battle between Guanghua and Patriotic is completely unrelated to the main point. Southeast Women's Physical Education Normal School Tenth Anniversary 238

Sports Performance—To Be Held Soon

The Southeast Women's Physical Education Normal School in Jiangwan has been established for ten years, with remarkable achievements. Now that it is the tenth anniversary, according to the school authorities, it was originally intended to expand the celebration to commemorate it. However, in the current national crisis, it is not what is desired. Therefore, the students' usual achievements in each subject will be performed in stages. The sports performance is scheduled for May 27th, the track and field sports meet is on June 3rd, and the commemorative ceremony will be held on the morning of the 14th, with a recreational meeting in the afternoon. A large number of people will visit at that time, so the school has agreed with the China General Omnibus Company that the No. 4 public bus will extend the closing time to 12 o'clock to facilitate transportation. It is also heard that the school authorities, in order to encourage the New Life Movement, will decline all gifts and congratulatory messages sent to the school to save expenses.

Education News

Elementary School Civics Courses Focus on Civic Morality 239

The Ministry of Education's Reply to the Hebei Provincial Government's Explanation

The Hebei Provincial Government recently consulted the Ministry of Education, stating that the Provincial Government meeting decided to request that primary and secondary schools increase moral education courses and requested a review and handling. The Ministry of Education replied to the Hebei Provincial Government yesterday, stating that, firstly, the training outline and specific items of the primary school civics course standards promulgated by the Ministry focus on the training of civic morality and strive for practice, which is more practical than the old moral education courses that only focused on lecturing. As for the secondary school civics course standards, they have been formulated by the Ministry and submitted to the Central Government for review and approval and will be announced soon.

This City's Elementary School Teacher Certification Begins Registration 241

Former Registered Personnel Who Should Take the Certification

The City Education Bureau is holding the third Elementary School Teacher Certification examination, and registration began on the 21st. After the registration deadline, a preliminary review will be conducted. Those who meet the qualifications for the examination and certification will be exempt from the written test. It is also reported that among the previously registered personnel, if those who registered with a certification qualification that has expired, or whose qualifications at the time of registration do not comply with Article 75 of the current Elementary School Regulations and need to be certified, should go to the Bureau to re-certify. It has been ordered to all elementary schools to inform teachers and staff accordingly.

Groundbreaking for New Provincial Shanghai Middle School Building 242

School Site Over 400 Mu, Construction Cost 700,000 Yuan

Requesting Education Commissioner of Jiangsu Province Zhou Fohai to Officiate at the Groundbreaking

Due to the small school site, unsuitable school buildings, and poor environment, the Provincial Shanghai Middle School in this city had plans to relocate and rebuild as early as five or six years ago. In recent years, with the efforts of Principal Zheng Xigu of the school and the support of provincial and municipal authorities and community members, steady progress has been made. Last winter, all procedures for selling the old school site and purchasing the new site were completed. This spring, architect Qi Minghe was commissioned to draw up plans for the new school buildings, and construction began in mid-March. Yesterday afternoon, a groundbreaking ceremony was held at the new school site in Wujia Lane on Hu-Min Road. Over two hundred people attended, including representatives of the school's faculty, staff, and students, as well as Commissioner Gu, representing Chairman Chen of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, Education Commissioner Zhou of the Jiangsu Education Department, Counselor Luo, representing Mayor Wu of the Shanghai Municipal Government, Bureau Directors Pan, Wu, and Wen, Director Xu, Magistrate Pan of Shanghai County, Section Chief Xue of the Provincial Education Department, and guests Ouyang Yuanhuai, Jiang Wenyu, Yao Mulian, He Bocheng, Lin Kanghou, Wang Zhixin, and others, totaling over fifty people. At 2:00 PM, the meeting commenced with music, followed by a ceremonial procession. Education Commissioner Zhou laid the foundation stone, and Principal Zheng delivered a speech, reporting on the process of relocation and rebuilding, and the points of effort that should be made in the future. Next, Education Commissioner Zhou delivered a speech, hoping that the school would pay attention to material construction, and at the same time, pay attention to spiritual training. Counselor Luo, Bureau Directors Pan, Wu, and Ouyang Yuanhuai, Jiang Wenyu, and Lin Kanghou then delivered speeches successively, with much encouragement in their words. The meeting concluded with a photo session at 4:30 PM. It is reported that the new school site covers a total of 450 mu, and the cost of purchasing the land, constructing the buildings, and equipping the facilities is approximately 700,000 yuan, truly a model for middle schools in the country. In the future, it is also planned to implement life education, and at the same time, use the school as the center of the community to promote compulsory education and engage in rural improvement.
