Free Talk

Making a Big Deal Out of a Small Thing 243

— Gong Yu

Big topics are difficult to tackle, and I'm too lazy to do them, so I can only do small topics; the outcome of small topics won't be big, and yet I yearn for something big, so I have to make a big deal out of a small thing.

The Eight-legged Essay examination for scholars, its essence is to cut out several small pieces from the classics, and ask the scholars to connect the meaning of the text, to become a kind of grand essay; but those who write grand essays in a vast and unrestrained manner are rejected, not only is it strenuous for the writer and taxing for the reader, but also everyone talks about "Now, of all things under heaven...", so wouldn't the world gradually become unstable from all the talking? Originally, there were ingenious methods for binding people's hearts and suppressing thought long ago.

However, once people are no longer selected based on essays, does the situation change? It's best not to talk, and don't even think, everyone should be leisurely. But if you must speak? The concession has Western prisons, the police have whips, the wilds have winding paths, the marshes have hesitation, letters are detained, newspapers have ink: ... how to stop it? You can still speak, but you're only allowed to say things like "leisurely," "refined," "subtle," "indirect": ... you're not allowed to say things like "Now, of all things under heaven"... In that case, is there no one left to speak about "the world"? In modern times, there seem to be quite a few. Talented people with golden words and embroidered mouths, experienced writers with imposing styles, are more beautiful than parrots and more skillful than monkeys. They still speak eloquently, with methods, and it's still "making a big deal out of a small thing."

For example, "There is a reason for the incident, but no evidence has been found," this kind of ingenious saying that doesn't touch the edges of things certainly seems very reasonable, but it has already buried right and wrong. Once the sense of right and wrong is lost, there is much more that can be said, so Jin Shengtan's head, and the heads of barbarians, are sold together: the ghosts of Yuan Zhonglang, X Zhonglang reappear in the world. What's more, wandering freely and treating all things equally, actually have emptiness and nothingness, messing around and trying to make oneself confused about everything. Fortunately, contemporary writers are not deeply rooted in antiquity, otherwise, they could bring out some bizarre and gaudy antiques to dazzle the ears and eyes of modern people.

But readers are often dissatisfied with small topics, so the other side has to make a big deal out of it. We only see "humor," "vulgar characters," "Western suits are not good to discuss": ... resounding in our ears, but they are all actually small topics, and the effort is really wasted.

On the Ping-Sui Railway Line 244

— Xu Ying

It is not comfortable to sit on the Ping-Sui train. In addition to the vibrations, the train also travels slowly.

Some people in Beiping who pull camels to carry heavy loads often make those two-humped animals proceed in strings on the railway tracks. The copper bells under the long whiskers jingle, and when the train comes, they unhurriedly walk away. It is said that the purpose of the copper bells is to scare away wolves.

Apart from the Zhengtai Railway, I am afraid that this is a relatively mountainous and dangerous road. The mountains are in the northern style, bald and completely naked, with large rocks jaggedly stretching out, and a dry landscape painted with dark brown and ginger yellow. Even in April, the ground is not green.

The train does not dare to go fast. One section is because the sleepers are already rotten, and going fast is feared to cause derailment; another section is where the train and the mountain form a right angle of ascent, and there is fear of sliding down halfway; another section is because there are quite a few passengers, and there is fear of decoupling. At one time, there was also the strange phenomenon of insufficient coal and water, but unfortunately I did not see it with my own eyes.

On this train, the armed comrades are always particularly numerous. Numerous but not amicable.

The first stop is Tsinghua Garden, the fifth station is Nankou... I don't need to waste ink repeating what everyone else says about these famous places. To put it simply, when you see more fruit trees, you are close to flat land. Reaching Kangzhuang, the following is flat and truly "Kang" (peaceful). Reaching "Huailai," you can see a vast expanse of orchards from afar.

The roadsides in Jiangnan are green and lush, fresh and full of vigor. Even if they are dilapidated, they still show striving. But in the north of the Great Wall, it is gray and dark, dry and lifeless. Everywhere there are bodies that have lost their souls, everywhere there is stark hunger and cold, houses that do not shelter from the wind and rain, hungry children, large eyes, thin faces.

Arriving at Datong, I particularly saw the cause of poverty. The land is full of sand, and some families rely on the transaction of "sex" for a living.

Around Datong, yellow winds blow almost every day, and sand and gravel obscure the sky, making even the steamed buns gritty. The water is also yellow and turbid. There is only one type of product in the sandy soil: potatoes (i.e., potatoes), which are the vegetables and food for most people, making their mouths feel sour when they eat them. If one day, the desert moves south to Datong, I am afraid that even potatoes will no longer be produced.

Who would willingly sell "sex" for a living? Here there are beautiful colors and small feet. What tears and blood are shed in the circumstances of "people below people"!

In the hot summer, perhaps you can see buckwheat fields, with the ears of wheat fluttering like swallows. Outsiders are not accustomed to eating pancakes made from this, because it is extremely purgative.

The train stops at Baotou, and there are no more railway tracks to the west.

The city of Baotou still has an ancient style. Although the imperialist's kerosene sells well, people still go to bed very early.

One day, I was sitting in a tall building drinking tea, and I saw in the street below a person dressed in formal attire pick up fresh horse manure from the road with his hand and put it in his bosom.

Dried horse manure can be burned as firewood without any smell. It is the only fuel in the Mongolian yurt.

Someone talked to me about going to the Mongolian yurt. You ride on your horse without dismounting, and shout, and if the host welcomes you, a woman will come and invite you to dismount, enter, and sit or lie down in a certain guest seat as you please. When eating, you eat together without having to thank or give money. When leaving, it is best to leave without saying goodbye, and they will not chase after you...

I am not very good at riding horses yet, so I stopped in Baotou and did not go further west.

Translation 245

— Gao Ping

After Reading the "Literary Works" Special Issue for March-May

"Literary Works" published a "Special Issue on the Literature of Small Nationalities" in March during this half-year period.

Most of the celebrities who recently belittle translation are those who understand foreign languages themselves and can read "the original," but the languages they understand are either English, French, German, or Russian. I'm afraid very few people understand Hungarian, Jewish, and Polish, right? If there were no English, German, or French translations, then how would our celebrities come into contact with the literature of small nationalities?

"Originalism" has misled many students in middle schools and universities, and frightened many readers in the arts and literature!

Our readers do not all understand foreign languages. Even if they have studied them, they only know one or two. However, they have the need to come into contact with world literature, and in addition to the literature of powerful countries, they also have the need to come into contact with the literature of small nationalities. Anyone with a little conscience cannot but admit that our own country's creations are still not as good as foreign works. "Stones from other mountains" should always be welcomed. If not, even if our country's creations are already better than foreign ones, we should still read foreign works, even if it's just to broaden our horizons and enrich our interests. Since we want to read foreign works, then the work of translation cannot be abolished, just as matchmakers are indispensable in an era when men and women do not have direct social interaction and cannot freely fall in love, if they want to get married.

There are also creative writers who look down on translation, because they are afraid that if readers focus too much on translation, they will inevitably "inflate the ambition of others and deflate our own prestige." This can also be used as evidence by drawing parallels to the example of domestic goods versus foreign goods. However, isn't the reason why domestic goods cannot resist foreign goods because domestic goods cannot imitate the manufacturing methods of foreign goods? The key to domestic goods should actually be to urge manufacturers to refer to the manufacturing methods of foreign goods and produce equally exquisite products. Otherwise, modern ladies will ultimately prefer to use imported goods. Economic resistance to the import of foreign goods has failed, but in the arts and literature, the closed-door policy toward foreign works has been highly effective. How can this be?

Lu Xun, who put a lot of effort into translation, once said this in a short essay: "Imagining how open-minded the Han people were, they did not hesitate to use newly arrived plants and animals to fill their decorative patterns. The Tang people were not considered weak either. For example, the stone beasts in front of the tombs of the Han people are mostly sheep, tigers, Tianlu, and Bixie, but on the Zhaoling tombs in Chang'an, there are carved galloping horses with arrows, and even an ostrich, which is simply unprecedented. Nowadays, not to mention on tombs, even in ordinary paintings, would anyone dare to use a foreign flower or a foreign bird? Even on private seals, would anyone be willing to use a cursive script or a vulgar character? Many refined people even use the sexagenary cycle to record the year, and only use the Republic of China era name when forced. I don't know if there are no artists with such boldness, or if there are any, but the people persecute them so much that they can only wither and die?

"The art and literature of the Song Dynasty had a national essence flavor that suffocated people, just like now. However, the Liao, Jin, and Yuan dynasties came in one after another. This news is worth pondering. Although the Han and Tang dynasties also had border troubles, their spirit was ultimately雄大. The people had the confidence not to be slaves to foreign races, or they didn't even think about it. Whenever they took foreign things, it was as if they had captured them and could freely drive them, without any concern. Once they became decadent and declined, their nerves became weak and sensitive. Whenever they encountered foreign things, they learned to look as if they had been captured by them, pushing away, panicking, retreating, escaping, shaking in a ball, and then they had to think up a reason to cover it up, and the national essence became the treasure of weaklings and weak slaves."

Although this passage is not about translation, it can be given to those who look down on translation. Those who insist that translation cannot be good have also made the mistake of making foreign things too frightening. In that short essay, Lu Xun also mentioned Yang Guangxian's opposition to Johann Adam Schall von Bell, saying, "Better to have no good calendar in China than to have Westerners in China." Some opponents of translation today actually have this kind of mentality.

On the reader's side, there are also those who dislike translation because the current translations are often not very fluent and do not look "爽快." In fact, there are various degrees of so-called fluency. Lin Qinnan's translation is generally considered to be fluent, but let us not talk about his "unfaithfulness," but only ask whether people who do not have a deeper cultivation of classical Chinese can "爽快" read Lin's translated novels? Similarly, people who say that the current translations are not 爽快 are actually not very clear about the grammar and structure of modern vernacular Chinese. Other people do not think they are not 爽快. Moreover, demanding fluency is not a proper attitude for readers. When we read ancient Chinese books, we also often encounter places that are not fluent, right? However, I have not heard people deny the value of ancient books because of this. There are also many great writers who imitate the profundity of ancient books, deliberately making them difficult to understand, thinking that they are capable!

In an era when translation work is being hampered to the point of almost complete stagnation, "Literary Works" has published two special issues on translation, which is really a very pleasant thing. The most powerful thing is that in these two special issues, the excellent translations provided answer the question of "Who should translate?" with ironclad proof. After reading Ivan's Misfortune, Twenty-Six and One, Change, Flute Melody in the Mountains in the March "Translation Special Issue" and In Prison, In the Public Security Bureau, Peach Garden, and Life-Taking Taishui in the May "Literature of Small Nationalities Special Issue," we can resolutely say that translators Zhou Jian, Chen Jie, Fen Jun, Zhang Luru, Bing Jia, Lian Suo, and Yu Sheng are the most worthy of the responsibility of translation. Their translations are simply like original creations, and in terms of content, they also make us believe that they are trustworthy, because no flaws can be found. What is especially worth noting is that the names of these translators are all names that we have never seen before. Perhaps there are some pen names of "veterans of the literary world" among them, but there must also be new translators, which is enough to make us very happy.

I believe that these two special issues of "Literary Works" will not be without influence on the Chinese literary world. At the very least, it makes readers believe that China has the above-mentioned excellent translators, and that many other translations can also give people a good impression. Chinese readers will definitely attach importance to translation because of this, and promote the work of translation, and have more contact with world literature, right?

However, "Literary Works" has not yet specifically answered the question of "What to translate?" I hope that "Literary Works" will not only be able to answer this question soon, but also be able to put it into practice soon. For example, many immortal masterpieces of the world have no one to translate, or even if they are translated, no bookstore is willing to print them. "Literary Works" may as well entrust people to translate them and serialize them, even if only one book can be serialized in a year.

Reminiscences 246

— Gao Bi

—Written in Commemoration of the Third Anniversary of the Death of My Old Friend Chen Xingshu—

(6) Xingshu's nature was very developed, but unfortunately he lost his loving mother as soon as he was born, which he regarded as an unforgettable regret for life. Although he had many brothers and sisters, overflowing with mutual warmth, it still could not reduce his longing for his mother. I had also lost my mother early on, and in my daily actions, I inevitably revealed some sadness. It was on this point that he felt a resonance, and he showed me extra warmth and understanding. In fact, my temperament was fundamentally different from his: I was taciturn and strong, he was gentle and tactful; I was willful in every way, he was tolerant in every way; I could not stand emotional agitation, and often made mistakes in speech, while he could use reason to regulate his emotions, allowing them to develop appropriately. Compared to the two of us, it should have been difficult to reconcile; however, although I myself was stubborn and willful, I very much hoped that others could give me some kind words of comfort, and the one who could comfort me the most was Xingshu; at the same time, I also saw that although Xingshu always took reason into account, he was actually full of rich emotions, and when reason and emotion clashed fiercely in his heart, it must have caused him pain and annoyance. I revealed this observation to him, and he fully agreed that I understood him. Our friendship became strong and firm under such mutual understanding.

I also had a strong aversion to Xingshu's extensive social interactions and his all-encompassing skills. I did indeed criticize him severely, and even openly denounced him as harboring dishonest thoughts and having terrible "means"—this was naturally a deliberate supervision, a kind of challenging oppression. Under such serious ridicule, he always looked extremely wronged, and used his unique tactful tone to explain his position—now that I think about it, how cruel I was—in the end, he cleverly said, "Even if I am a person who is good at using "means," I would not use "means" on you." I accepted this famous sentence very satisfactorily.

I remember once, he was sitting silently in thought, and Zhongchi and I strolled over, and he suddenly said to me, "If possible, what would you hope for in the general public's perception of you?" I frankly said, "I hope that everyone can respect and fear me. That's all. What about you?" I asked him in return. He smiled and said, "I am the same as you, except that I would change the word "respect and fear" to "love" instead." At that time, Zhongchi said directly from the side, "This is the difference in your ideas; that is also the dividing line of your actions."

Now there is one thing that my old friend should know, and that is: in the past, he often advised me to restrain my emotions with words of gold and jade. Although I also had the intention of accepting it at the time, I always thought it was a kind of training in "worldly wisdom" and had nothing to do with the grand purpose of establishing oneself. Now I understand that this was my great misunderstanding. If a person does not do some analytical work in reason, but just goes straight forward and expresses himself in a general way, the result will either be ignorance or deception; this is clearly an unsound consciousness, in other words, it is a great flaw in life. When I think of the many damnable emotional behaviors of the past, I am truly ashamed and without ground, and alas, today's change cannot be praised by Xingshu.

Corpse 247

— Zhang Yiping

A Gen held sesame cakes and returned to the store, and many tea customers had already arrived.

There is no need to introduce them one by one, they are all those familiar faces that do not change in wind and rain. The people who can show their faces a little in this Five Families Town are all gathered here.

If it weren't for some kind of fierce general meeting or something, there wouldn't be any strange faces discovered in Fuxing Tea Garden; a person who rarely sets foot in the tea garden who wants to come here for a rest, first of all has to be served by those comrades in long gowns who consider themselves masters—those who wear long gowns in Five Families Town are all people of status—and their eyes are rotating on your face with question marks, huh! Can you also come to the tea garden to chat grandly?

Speaking of A Gen, he is naturally busy serving tea and water, and his feet are always paddling in the mud, and he is thinking about the loss of two big oceans in his heart. He foolishly thinks it is a joke, Zhu Master has not died, outside the door, isn't he? Hey, Zhu big officer, that, Zhu Master must not have died.

"Zhu big officer, Zhu Master has not come?" A Gen was stunned by the two dollars and shouted it out.

Zhu big officer was covered in sweat, and his body was like a swing, with no place to rest. He didn't even call out uncle or elder to so many elders and fathers,

He pushed aside the welcoming A Gen and asked headlessly;

"Have you seen him?"

Old Master Xu is after all sitting in the first seat in Five Families Town. Whoever dares to say no to his ideas, no, his orders, will really not be able to handle it. However, anyone in this Five Families Town can die, but Zhu Xiaoquan can't be without eyes. Old Master Xu almost forgot to eat the sesame cakes, and was planning on this matter of ordering. Zhu Second Officer, that fellow, is not easy to mess with. He doesn't understand what elders and fathers are, let alone the authority of those sitting in the first seat. He talks about fists, and if he kills someone, he can open a pier. If he catches him, he can also say that in twenty years he will be a good man again. What Old Master Xu is most afraid of are good men, because a good man's two fists are not like A Gen's, which often hit his own buttocks. Old Master Xu has been eating three sesame cakes every day for many years, but he has never eaten a fist; however, he is sitting in the first seat in Five Families Town, and if a fist comes flying at his face, he has to move his own face forward to meet it, so A Gen's loss of two dollars for Zhu Xiaoquan's death is in no way as worrisome as one ten-thousandth of Old Master Xu's concern. Zhu big officer has come, "Have you seen him?" It seems that "his" fist is waving in front of Old Master Xu's face, but Old Master Xu, who is sitting in the first seat, cannot but issue an order.

Grains, Flour, and Wheat Remain Sluggish and Depressed 261

Wheat prices experienced a sluggish trend across all months after yesterday's futures market opened. Imported wheat quotations retreated by 10 to 20 cents. Although the weather was variably cloudy and sunny, the climate was very good. According to news from various inland gangs, the new wheat harvest is expected to begin in about a week, with a flourishing market in three weeks. Judging from the current situation, there is a strong indication of a bumper harvest. Given the flat sales of flour and the inability to replenish new goods, the market is expected to continue to decline in the future. As a result, July fell by one cent from the previous day, August fell by three cents, and September fell by three cents. Spot wheat remained flat. As new wheat is about to enter the market, sources of old wheat from various regions continued to arrive. Yesterday, another three to four thousand bags of wheat arrived via the Jinpu Railway. According to estimates by industry members, even after the new wheat is released, old wheat will continue to arrive. It was reported that over four packages of rail wheat from various regions were handled by Fuxin. The market situation stabilized.

Flour: After the flour market opened yesterday morning, all months initially showed signs of fatigue followed by stability. Imported wheat quotations fell by about 10 to 20 cents in Chicago and about 15 cents in Canada. Therefore, after the opening, market prices for all months were down by one cent or 7.5 cents compared to the previous day. Later, as factories did not sell, the market lacked sufficient chips. External bears made slight adjustments. Afterwards, opening prices showed slight stability again. In the afternoon, the market situation for all months generally consolidated, with very few sales. Although factories were willing to sell, the market lacked buyers, making sales difficult. For example, although the Yingkou Gang moved the previous day, it remained on the sidelines yesterday, indicating that the actual purchasing power was still dismal. As a result, May and June fell by 7.5 cents, July rose by 5 cents, and August, September and October were unchanged.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Essays

A Word to Our Country's Far Eastern Games Athletes 267

— Jiasheng

The 10th Far Eastern Games concluded yesterday (May 20th). Our country, apart from maintaining the football championship and Chen Baoqiu winning second place in the shot put and Fu Baolu winning second place in the pole vault in track and field, all other championships in ball games, track and field, swimming, etc., were won by Japan and the Philippines. It is conceivable that our country's performance cannot catch up with the Far East! Now I understand that our country's delegation will return home on the Jackson steamship the day after tomorrow (23rd). I am 120,000% willing to expose my naked heart to the delegation and hope they will pay attention to this little article of mine.

The reasons why our country's performance is not as good as Japan and the Philippines can be summarized into two points:

(1) Regarding innate factors:

I remember a certain Mr. coming to our school last year to give a lecture. He said, "The result of the Third National Games held in Hangzhou was that Liu Changchun and Sun Guiyun were a great sensation, and the whole country admired them. However, after investigating the reasons why they had special achievements in running, I discovered that their ancestors had to run dozens of miles every day in the past, that is, from their homes to other places to do business. Their ancestors had an instinct for running stored in their cells, and this instinct was passed on to later generations. Their descendants are undoubtedly famous runners!" Although we cannot completely trust what Mr. said, at least the development of innate instincts has considerable value. We only need to observe the physique of Westerners and Chinese on the road to know that heredity is not false.

By analogy, our country's backwardness and the lack of innate heredity are undeniable. The only way to remedy this is to temper our physique and move towards a state of health and strength, hoping that our next generation will have a healthy physique and compete with foreign countries again. Japan's improvement in physique is a lesson from the past.

The innate strengths of Japanese and Filipino athletes are stronger, while the innate strengths of our country's athletes are weaker, resulting in backward performance, which we can forgive.

(2) Regarding acquired factors:

The success of any event is never accidental. It requires long-term training and spiritual cultivation. Now, let's discuss them separately:

(A) Long-term training:

This is probably a common problem among our country's athletes! Anyone who has shown some talent in sports does not practice regularly. Only a few weeks before the World Games, the Far Eastern Games, the District Games, the Jiangda Games, the School Games, and the group competitions do they begin to practice. After a long period of cessation, suddenly practicing intensely, can their performance improve? Even if it improves, its rate is definitely not as fast as regular, long-term practice. Therefore, I hope that in the future, athletes will have long-term training and never resort to temporary cramming.

(B) Spiritual Cultivation:

Without spiritual cultivation, the physique cannot be healthy, and performance is even more out of the question! To be honest, Chinese athletes are really lacking in spiritual cultivation. Dance halls, cinemas, cafes..., are full of their traces. Pursuing the opposite sex is their wish. Such destruction of the body and wasting of energy cannot but lead to backward performance. On the one hand, we cannot deny that this is due to the social environment, but who dares to deny their weak will? I hope that in the future, athletes will thoroughly correct their past mistakes and pay attention to spiritual cultivation. This will not only make great progress in performance but also extend our lifespan!

As for other reasons, such as conflicts of opinion among athletes, incorrect selection criteria, and the scattered residence of athletes, lack of contact, etc., are secondary reasons and will not be mentioned.

In conclusion: Regarding innate aspects, although we are not as good as Japan, the Philippines, and other strong nations, if we can fully cultivate and restrain ourselves in acquired aspects, our performance will definitely not be so backward. I hope to witness our athletes at the 11th Far Eastern Games raising their eyebrows and exhaling, defeating foreign races, and winning the championship back, fighting for a breath of fresh air for the motherland. That is what the author prays for sincerely.

On the Issue of Students Smoking 268

— Jingjia

Yesterday's newspaper education news had a piece saying: "The Ministry of Education issued a circular to schools in all provinces and cities, strictly prohibiting students from smoking." This made me feel deeply emotional!

In recent years, cigarettes have become an extremely popular and widespread consumer product. Most young people smoke. Some people even think that not smoking is not being a modern person. Therefore, some people who don't smoke often pick up a cigarette and play with it, as if they are puffing clouds. In schools, these phenomena are extremely common.

Not only that, but smoking foreign goods is not enough to show off wealth. In the eyes of smoking students, the best domestic cigarettes are no match for the worst foreign cigarettes. In other words, it is better to send money abroad.

How terrible are these phenomena! If this continues, on the one hand, students' psychology will become increasingly bad, and on the other hand, economic leakage will be even greater. The consequences are unimaginable!

On this point, strictly prohibiting students from smoking is undoubtedly a benevolent policy!

However, doubt follows! The regulations of every school have rules prohibiting smoking, and at the same time, there is no school without smoking students! How are these contradictory phenomena produced? Moreover, on the negative side, people who smoke in society are not all from schools. Even if they don't smoke in school, they will smoke after entering society! Does it mean that they can smoke immediately after leaving student life?

If it is said that students are too young to smoke because it is harmful to their health. But we know that arsenic can kill old people and young people at the same time. Why are we so concerned about the health of students and so dismissive of people outside the student body?

The words seem too crooked, and the meaning is inevitably "distorted." However, can prohibiting students from smoking be effective with just a circular? I can say categorically, no!

Any circular cannot resist the power of temptation!

Under the call of the New Life Movement, the emergence of these circulars is inevitable. However, I ask the education authorities to pay attention to another point! Students who dance all night in dance halls, cinemas, and fancy restaurants, holding women, are filling the schools. I dare not believe that these behaviors are more noble than smoking.

I don't advocate smoking—although I smoke myself—and I don't object to issuing circulars strictly prohibiting students from smoking. However, I hope:

(1) Pay attention to student behavior that is worse than smoking.

(2) Improve the environment in the student world; reduce bad temptations.

Small Goldfish 269

— Yingying

In front of the writing desk, there is a large glass high-footed tank. It holds many small goldfish.

From the outside of the tank, those aquatic animals inside are so small and agile!

Crowding, squeezing past the shoulders of companions, and swimming past the tails of other companions!

They never stop for a moment; they are like small swimming

Page 18

experts, with extremely persistent endurance!

Green and lush fine grass set off a pair of goldfish of the same golden color; swimming together so intimately like a pair of little lovers.

There is one that is all black! Only the middle of the belly has a layer of white, which is relatively longer, like an older brother in the team.

There is also a golden-red one, with a butterfly girl's wing-shaped tail!

Four adorable little companions do nothing all day but compete to learn to swim, hoping that a good ambition can be realized to become a swimmer.

Snowy younger brother comes home from school. First, he throws away his schoolbag and looks at his little friends to see if they are safe and lively? He also shares some of the small cakes that his mother gave him to eat.

He says that if they don't eat, they won't swim! If they don't swim, they won't be fun anymore.

The innocent little heart doesn't understand how to call death? He only knows that if they don't move, they will no longer be of interest!

Each time, he must see them himself before he can rest assured! Then he reviews his lessons and writes.

But unfortunately, the fact will really come one day!

As usual, he came home from school. He generously scattered some of the small bread that his sister gave him into the glass tank!

Suddenly, he cried.

"What's wrong, Xuexue?" Mom asked him.

"It's not good, Mom, the little goldfish aren't moving—they don't want to eat the sweet bread."

I don't know when these little lives died!

"Xuexue, the little goldfish are all dead! Of course, they won't eat your sweet bread."

"How did they die? I don't want them to die, I want them to eat the sweet bread I gave them!"

"If they're dead, how can they live! We'll buy a few more tomorrow, and you hide the sweet bread. Let Huahua eat these for dinner."

"Swallow them like that? Ah, no way. Huahua is not guilty?"

He hurriedly opened a cigarette case. He gently scooped the dead goldfish into the box. Teary-eyed, his eyes swollen like the protruding eyes of the dead goldfish, looking pitiful! The child's heart is the most kind—he buried those poor little lives!

The Concrete Future of Chinese Women 270

— Ms. Xiuying

After reading the article "The Future of Chinese Women" in the 19th issue of this journal, I deeply sympathize with the author, Mr. Boer, and believe that the article's arguments are much more intelligent and correct than the general empty calls for women's movement and all kinds of flamboyant propositions. Now, I will also try to write a few opinions, and if they can be connected with the previous article, then my humble opinions to female comrades are as follows:

First, objective facts have already shown that the so-called "women's suffrage movement" and "free love" are slogans of the past. It is true that women needed such liberation when overthrowing the old shackles of habits and systems. However, nowadays, many frivolous young men and women of the leisure class have turned "free love" into a "love of money" style of prostitution on the streets; at the same time, the meaning of "political participation movement" has become an activity phenomenon of the special class of "wives gaining status through their husbands":::::. All of this is not a sufficient warning to us that the so-called "current women's movement should change slogans"? Moreover, the following women's movement cannot but adopt a more advanced policy. Therefore, we believe that the foundation of women's equal love must be established in the process of production and labor to build life; women's political sovereignty must create their own position in the struggle to overthrow the exploiting class and all those who regard women as appendages or decorations. Only in this way can women fight for freedom and equality!

Second, regarding physical and mental strength, it is natural that women lack opportunities for development due to historical constraints. However, now we should train in actual operating habits. On the one hand, we must resolutely oppose the leisure class's idle and boring "promoting women's education" or flamboyant "women's health," etc., contempt, and slogans of women playing with women. Because the facts tell us that the current general education and physical education trends, at least in China under this feudal restraint and imperialist oppression, are undoubtedly a kind of clothing to decorate the ruling class, and even a kind of anesthetic to fool the public. We have seen countless female graduates of large and small schools who can neither do things for society nor take care of daily family life, and even cannot handle the necessary operations for their own lives - then, is this because their brains are subject to autocratic restrictions? Or is it that their physiques are not healthy at all? Heaven knows! They only cultivate their physical strength to specialize in efforts to make the opposite sex sensual; at the same time, they use their mental strength to cater to the masturbatory or buying and selling skills of their lovers. Therefore, in order to respect women's rights, women should now train their mental strength in understanding society and enriching knowledge! They should train their physical strength in operational skills (from factories to kitchens, they should be attentive!), only in this way can the true virtues of women be expressed.

Third, according to the "establishment of women's struggle standards in the objective environment" mentioned in the first point above and the "establishment of women's solid strength in subjective quality" mentioned in the second point; finally, the women's movement should be regarded as war, in strategy, all those who oppress or trample on women of the leisure class (not only men punching and kicking people, but also using power and profit to force women to marry, or rape, etc., also belong to oppression and trampling) and their systems should be regarded as enemies. All those who labor for the welfare of the public (regardless of mental or physical strength) and the goals they desire should be regarded as friendly forces, so that the task of the women's movement can be completed. This is an extremely clear path, just like the strategy of the world women's movement, in the weak Chinese ethnic group, it should overthrow the great powers and unite all the weak ethnic groups, which is a fighting formation!

In conclusion: The future of women has reached the forefront of social movements. The struggle for liberation is as urgent as the current actual productive forces need a new production system suitable for their own development. (Rewarded)

Biography of Frustration (8) 271

— Forget Myself

Wife's Friends

Return Journey 272

— Boer

A loud and long whistle, pressing, urging, driving people away. One by one, they began to roll around, like a tide, rushing in all directions, wolfishly and turbulently.

The ship gradually began to move, and the waves behind its stern hit countless white swirls, rolling, splashing, and clumps of water flowers, soaring into the sky.

With a final "woo," the ship finally left the dock, and my six months of life in H city were over.

For me, the journey is nothing but a boring thing. Who wants to put boredom in their liver?

Bored, I stood on the deck, looking at the green sky, the endless coastline, bathing in the sunlight, splashing with seawater, and the cool sea breeze swept across my face. I immediately felt an infinite sense of ease and pleasure.

But soon after, a lofty sense of worry still lurked deeply in my heart. The road of life is a long run without end, isn't my future as vast as the ocean?

For the sake of education, whipped by the iron chains of life—allow me to say it so bluntly—I must wander everywhere...

At this moment, I feel empty, unfamiliar, lonely, contradictory... The earth is always messy, dirty, and lifeless. I am unfamiliar with my family, and I am also unfamiliar with society. I feel that I am living alone in this cold society, and I do not feel any enthusiasm, kindness, or cooperative emotions.

Bearing the heavy burden of a history of trauma, I stagger through hardship, and the road is getting farther and farther.

Sadly, I sighed, shook my body, and wiped the small beads of seawater splashing on my face.

At this time, a Ph.D. in law who had just returned from the United States and voluntarily introduced himself to me patted me on the shoulder and said;

"Mr., aren't you very lonely? The whole of China is lonely, and it's terrible. I also regret coming back to the messed-up China."

"Why?" I coldly asked him his name. He opened his eyes and said;

"China is not good, not good. Look: dirty, messy, corrupt, despicable, barbaric... It's simply not worthy of being called a civilized country! Mr., the United States is different. They are rich in creativity, living, and everything is on track. No wonder they are a rich country and a strong people... I dare to say boldly that the United States is a paradise and China is a hell. Mr., would you believe me?"

"I don't want to hear you make such a judgment..."

"So, you don't think I'm right?"

To be honest with you, Mr., if China wants to be strong, it can only follow the United States. I think we must cooperate with the United States, otherwise China will never have hope."

I gave him a cold glance, and couldn't help but laugh secretly in my heart. I thought this was a foreign Ph.D., a university professor, one of the guides of the country's highest culture, talking nonsense. Wasn't China poisoned by people like them? So I bluntly said to him;

"Dr., how can you not change into a Chinese, that yellow face can never be washed off? I hope you, very much, open your eyes wide, calmly study the real China, the real situation of the world, and then make a judgment, and then discuss, but, never forget that you are also a Chinese!"

He hummed from his nose and said to me angrily, "You don't understand! You don't understand! You have no manners!" Then he ran away quickly.

Woo! The whistle sounded twice, and I also ran back to my room. My heart was still lonely, but there was some amusement.

Travel Notes and Essays 273

— He Juefu

Following humor, travel notes and essays seem to be taking the upper hand in the literary world. If we casually flip through an American newspaper or magazine, we can find this type of article at any time; moreover, some publications even rely solely on this to make a living.

There are likely hardships for authors in today’s mass production of travel notes and essays. The hardship is probably due to being born in this chaotic world. They are unwilling to pledge allegiance to power (or have no way to curry favor), writing flattering articles like slaves. They are also afraid of guns and knives, daring not to openly resist and write great works that correct the world and people’s hearts. If they were to remain silent and not ask about worldly affairs, not only would they feel unhappy inside, but they would also worry about solving the problem of three meals a day. Therefore, they have to choose this path and run along with it. The trend of pure conversation in the Jin Dynasty was extremely popular for a time, and the small essays of the late Ming Dynasty were able to sweep the world, perhaps for the same reason. Living in a turbulent and uneasy China, especially in this metropolis full of coal smoke, people's spiritual lives are extremely oppressed and uncomfortable. Not having the opportunity to go to high mountains and great rivers to see scenic spots, to relax and enjoy a breath of fresh air, and to become a hermit in deep forests and famous mountains is even more impossible. Therefore, lying in a small room, reading travel notes and essays of famous people, one can also gain a moment of leisure and comfort. Quenching thirst by thinking of plums is the same principle.

People need a little comfort. However, will the comfort gained from these travel notes and essays cause people to become muddled and estranged from the real world? No one dares to say.

The trend of small essays from the late Ming Dynasty, which had been buried for two or three hundred years, now seems to have signs of revival. Originally, the Spirit School of the late Ming Dynasty, which did not force a strong interest, did not follow ancient methods, and expressed its own views without imitating the ancients, had a very correct perspective. A faithful writer must do this. Even if it is promoted now, hundreds of years later, it does not lose its original value. However, it is a pity that the current group of authors has tainted the predecessors' propositions and greatly imitated their works.

I remember Lu Xun saying in his article "The Crisis of Small Essays": A surviving small essay must be a dart, a throwing spear, something that can kill a bloody path to survival together with the readers. We do not not need small essays now, but we are dissatisfied with not being able to find darts and throwing spears of this kind now.

Fiction

MADAM X (2) 274

— Dai Ni

"Mr. Wang received our letter?" Mrs. Beiping smiled.

"I came here as soon as I received it. I haven't seen Junyang for three years." But in his heart he thought - he really has her! That guy who doesn't understand women!

"Junyang often talks about Mr. Wang, a handsome man." She laughed like a silver bell, but it was so natural, a Mrs. Beiping who could make Junyang breathe in front of urban women.

"Junyang is always joking, he's just kidding." He raised his body slightly to speak, but Caulmen's eyeballs were glancing at Chaplin's hair, Heifetz's nose and mouth, and the snow-white silk scarf corner on his collar in the mirror of the opposite wardrobe.

-- A handsome man? A group of urban women, red-lipped young ladies, dancers in high heels surrounding him, but "who would love them"! No girl has the manager of the World Trading Company Mr. Min Sun's Caulmen's eyeballs.

Retracting his gaze to see the other party smiling charmingly, he glanced at the corner of the silk scarf on his collar again, smoking a cigarette, maintaining a gentleman's attitude.

"Mr. Wang, is something wrong?" Mrs. Beiping misunderstood.

"No!" Slightly shaking Chaplin's hair, expressing such politeness, "Junyang is probably coming back soon, right?"

"He went to find a few friends, maybe to the World Trading Company. He knows Mr. Wang has arrived here. He will definitely come back!"

When the second cigarette was offered warmly, there was a slight knock on the door outside.

"Junyang is back." Min Sun almost lost his gentlemanly demeanor and jumped up.

Mrs. Beiping walked with light steps, fluttering like a goddess. Opening the door, a waiter in white uniform said humbly:

"Madam, there's a phone call."

Mrs. Beiping turned around, "Mr. Wang, please wait a moment."

"Please go ahead."

Standing up to see Mrs. Beiping out the door, Min Sun paced in the room. He saw a handsome man walking everywhere in the room: Chaplin's hair, Caulmen's eyeballs, Heifetz's nose and mouth, and the snow-white silk scarf corner.

-- That guy, tricking a beautiful woman back to Shanghai, he really has it! But thinking of his waving "I'm heartbroken!" he couldn't help but smile in a Heifetz style; he immediately restrained his smile as if his secret had been discovered, straightened his tie in the mirror, and returned to his original seat, sitting upright with such politeness.

In front of Mrs. Beiping, he discovered his own insignificance.

The sound of disciplined high-heeled leather shoes approached the door, the lady was obviously a skilled dancer. - That guy must have come from sitting in cafes, right?

"Mr. Wang, what a joke! Junyang said he was held back by friends and couldn't get away; I said isn't Mr. Wang your friend? People have been here for half a day, there must be something going on!"

Film Special Issue The Shun Pao Screen Section Wednesday, May 23, Year 23 of the Republic of China

The Dismissal Incident of Renowned Soviet Film Director Room Shocks the Soviet Film Industry 275

— Xun Zhi

On March 19 of this year, the Soviet People's Committee's Film Industry Main Affairs Bureau swiftly and decisively dismissed A.M. Room, a first-class Soviet director, from his position in the film industry. At the same time, it was decided to hand him over to the inquiry committee for deliberation. This incident shocked the entire Soviet film industry, and its impact even spread to countries around the world. In the Soviet Union, there are currently only five technicians with the honor of first-class director: (1) Eisenstein (K.S.E.) of "Battleship Potemkin" and "The Old and the New," (2) Ms. Schub of "Four Women" (Esther Svhub), (4) Ermler of "Fragment of an Empire" and "Counterplan," and Room, whom we are going to talk about here, who became famous with "The Great Undertaking." In the Soviet Union, first-class directors have the greatest authority and reputation. They can choose scripts according to their own wishes and freely produce films. Therefore, the dismissal of a first-class director is undoubtedly a major event in the Soviet film industry this year. In the early 1920s, Room successively produced famous works such as "Death Bay," "The Spy," and "Third Meshchanskaya Street." "Bed and Sofa" is his representative successful work. In 1930, he completed the Soviet Union's first and also the greatest artistic sound film "The Great Undertaking." His reputation and the momentum of his new talent were not inferior to Pudovkin and Eisenstein. The reason for this dismissal was lax work and waste of public funds. Since "The Great Undertaking," he had been resting for more than two years. Until February 1933, he began planning a new work. Initially, it was scheduled to be prepared from February to May, and filming would be completed from May to the following May. However, during this period, Room never decided on a filming plan, never wrote a complete filming script, and worked with a vague and directionless attitude. As of February 1 of this year, out of the planned production cost of 600,000 rubles, a total of 509,000 rubles had been spent, while only 5% of the entire film had been completed. Therefore, the 17th Congress of the Soviet Party determined that Room's behavior was bureaucratic contempt of responsibility, which could not be tolerated during the second Five-Year Plan's shock process. It was decided to revoke his position and hand him over for punishment as a warning to all film practitioners. On March 19, the above decision was announced in the name of Shumyatsky, Chairman of the Main Affairs Bureau. At the same time, it was also decided that Shvinnikov, Director of Artistic Production of the Moscow Film Studio, was negligent in supervision, and Metalnikov, Director of the Moscow Combined Film Factory, was inept in handling affairs, and they were given reprimands. The Room incident is quite similar to the Pudovkin reprimand incident last year. Because Pudovkin began filming the new film "Deserter" the year before last. This film was based on the German workers' movement. Later, due to the drastic changes in the objective situation in Germany, the content was repeatedly reshot, so that the original film consumed 400,000 feet, and the production date was extended to more than two years. After the film was made, although it had unique artistic qualities, it had quite a few errors in its point of view. Therefore, in order to clarify responsibility, the Film Industry Main Affairs Bureau also imposed a reprimand. From the above two incidents, we can know the organization and control of the Soviet film industry, as well as the poignant and tragic emotions of film practitioners in the second Five-Year Plan.

Audience Opinions

After Seeing "Good Night" 276

— Wang Benxi

It has great significance, why use eroticism?

The actors all have considerable achievements and are beyond reproach.

Tan Ying plays the young widow with profound expressions, bringing to life a young girl who, although under the oppression of the old etiquette, has a quiet heart that seeks the nourishment of spring. Tan Ying's achievements after changing her style far exceed her previous works. However, her willow-like eyebrows and permed hair are incompatible with the identity of the character in the play. Although this issue has been corrected many times, it is ultimately not noticed by the production authorities. The several erotic scenes also feel unnecessary. A great work has its own great significance, why use eroticism?

Finally, I believe that if works such as "Pear Blossoms in the Rain" and "Good Night" can be used with sound, it will further enhance the emotions in the play. Although the subtitles of this film are also concise and moving, they are not as strong as sound.

Thoughts After Seeing "Good Night" 277

— Xu Meilan

A Woman's Cry

After watching this film, I couldn't help but have a feeling.

Does etiquette really devour people? I have doubted this question for many years. Now, in "Good Night," it has very clearly answered me. It says: "Etiquette is going to eat people, especially us women."

Under the principle of monogamy, husband and wife should mutually maintain chastity. If the wife dies, the husband remarries. Then, if the husband dies, the wife remarries, it is undoubtedly a proper and appropriate thing. However, our country's so-called etiquette does not allow it. It only allows a man to remarry after his wife dies, but a woman cannot remarry after her husband dies. She should observe chastity for her deceased husband. In order to reward such chaste women, chastity arches are produced. May I ask, what is the significance of this chastity? This is obviously to destroy us women. Under this cruel and inhumane system, I don't know how many tens of millions of my female compatriots' lives have been devoured over the years. Under the solemn and sacred chastity arches recognized by a group of people, I don't know how many lively souls of my female compatriots have been suppressed. What a tragic and unjust thing this is!

Now is the time for us to rise up and resist. For the sake of our own future happiness, we can no longer succumb to this inhumane and unreasonable system. We should unite and fight this man-eating etiquette, to melee. We must use the greatest courage to defeat her, to redeem our freedom and happiness.

Female compatriots, it is useless to wipe tears with silk handkerchiefs after watching "Good Night"!

Norma Shearer's masterpiece "The Divorcee" - Starting Thursday at the Grand Theater 278

Homeless Sacrifice 279

— Si Tong

Written after watching "Good Night"

In fact, feudal forces and old etiquette are still deeply rooted. They bind the hearts of many people, destroy and bury many precious lives. Although since the May Fourth Movement, a part of society has been liberated (in fact, it is just replacing feudal forces and old etiquette with decadence, romance, and carnal desire... It is still far from liberation, which is most heartbreaking.) But except for a few big cities and a few places with open customs, most compatriots are still groaning under this pressure. Therefore, the anti-feudal movement should continue to be carried out to seek the final victory and move towards a bright future. The appearance of "Good Night" is precisely to inject a shot of morphine into the struggling people. We cannot say that its intention has lost the spirit of the times. This is a point that should be clearly recognized.

However, the final result in this film is not satisfactory. Zhu Ying gave twelve points of sympathy to Yun Lin's environment, and repeatedly said "rescue her from the fire pit" and "break the shackles of etiquette"...; Yun Lin and her grandmother Liu Jiemu disappeared their youth under various pressures; and the descriptions of the clan chief, villains, and hypocrites, and the exposure of crimes, etc.; in the end, they can only give them minor verbal punishments, and Liu Jiemu even sacrificed herself, which is beyond the audience's expectations and makes people feel unfair. In this way, hypocrites and thugs get victory instead, and the weak are still weak in the end. It fails to indicate a clear path to the countless Liu Jiemu and Yun Lin now. Therefore, Liu Jiemu's sacrifice and Yun Lin's lack of belonging only give people more material for a sigh.

Written after watching "Two Against One" 280

— Nai Huang

If you have seen "Sisters," and then go to see "Two Against One," then you must shout that you have been wronged, and say that Mingxing became rich and then messed things up.

Because the consciousness of this film is fundamentally wrong. As for the football field, it is messed up, and the confusion when kicking the ball is the worst.

As for the actors, there is really no place to show their strengths, and they are not very hardworking. Wang Xianzhai and others are completely disappointing.

There are also a few actresses who are too contrived, so they are also very disappointing.

In short, this film is the worst production of Mingxing this year, far worse than "Sisters." It is hoped that the Mingxing authorities will carefully investigate future productions, otherwise their credibility will be lost.

"Wine, Sex, Wealth, and Temper" Grand Hotel 281

All ten interior scenes of Lianhua Second Factory's new film "Wine, Sex, Wealth, and Temper" can be said to be great. Recently, the interior scene of the corridor on the upper floor of the hotel, which is being filmed, is only the so-called passing scene in the play. However, under the Lianhua production principle of not being sloppy, "the set with not many shots was built in six days and nights of continuous work, covering an area of more than fifty square feet. The elevators, escalators, rooms, and corridors are all completely lifelike, and the style and decoration are even more modernized. It is said that when designing this set, set designer Liu Jin San Jun visited more than a dozen new-style hotels in Shanghai and consulted many architectural drawings for reference.

The entire play is full of tension and sorrow. Tianyi Company once selected this film to participate in this year's National Domestic Film Competition. Film Novel

Wonder Bar (6) 283

— Shu Ming

The black people's song and dance program in Heaven is very extensive. After Al finished his own singing, he hurried to see Inez. Inez was crying in her dressing room. She said that Harry must have been killed by her. Al laughed at her and said she was crazy. Harry was just hurt, and he has already gone home with Captain Flynn. By tomorrow, everything will be fine. As he spoke, he gently put a shawl around her shoulders, thinking about how to comfort her later and make her forget about Harry. His heart was full of hope. He wanted to come back after everything was over and tell her how much he loved her. He wanted to take her home himself. But when he went out for a while, when he came back, Tommy was already in Inez's dressing room. Tommy saw Al and quickly called him in. Al went in, but seeing that the two of them were both younger than him and showing a sense of light pity and affection, he couldn't help but feel a little embarrassed. He saw that Inez's face was still covered with a lot of makeup oil, so he said: "Be careful of the oil on your face, it will stick you together." When Inez heard this, she handed a towel to Tommy. Tommy quickly took it and happily wiped the oil on her face for her. While wiping, he said: "Honey, isn't this the same as before?" He also explained to Al: "I always wiped the oil on her face before. It's been a long time since I wiped it."

Al saw that expression and couldn't help but feel uncomfortable, so he said to Inez: "I'll take you home in a while. Breathe some fresh air on the road, and you'll definitely feel better." But they were silent for a while, and then Inez said: "Okay, you are too good to me." Tommy stood up and said: "Good is good, but, Al, I have composed a new song and want to play it for her. Let me take her back." Inez unknowingly took Tommy's hand. Al pretended not to care and said: "That's fine too." Inez said: "Walk with us, okay?" Tommy also said: "That's great, you come and walk with us." Al smiled. His face was black because he hadn't taken off his makeup yet, covering the pain in his heart, because his hopes were all in vain now. He understood in his heart that the two young people were pitying him, an old man, and adding kindness. But he still pretended to be nonchalant and smiled: "Sitting and listening to two children singing mountain songs? I can't do it." He walked towards the door. He said: "I wish you happiness." This was really his sincere blessing, but unknowingly his shoulders slumped down.

A night of singing and dancing was over. The tables were empty. The red and green streamers were broken. The flowers in the bottles were dry. A tired opera singer was wiping off some of the black oil left on his face. He was the last one to walk out of the Wonder Bar. The lights in the hotel were extinguished one by one, revealing the gradually brightening fish-belly white of the East. A newsboy was already shouting extras. Al bit his lip and waved to the newsboy. He bought an extra. When he opened the newspaper, his heart was pounding and beating unevenly. Then he took a deep breath. Nothing happened. Inez was fine. But he shouldn't let her know. The headline on the newspaper was: "Captain Flynn and famous dancer Harry died tragically in a car accident." (End)
